   - Extend `verify_sentence_to_record(...)` to set `evaluator_agrees=verifier_pass` on every constructed `VerifiedSentence` (rule-based "agrees with itself"; meaningful when a future Issue replaces this populator with a real two-family LLM judge). This is where actual generator-path `VerifiedSentence` objects get their fields, per Codex iter 2.

### Frontend

   - Add `evaluator_agrees: boolean | null` to `ReportVerifiedSentence` interface.

6. `web/app/generation/components/sentence_inspector.tsx`
   - Add `AgreementBadge({ sentence })` component:
     - `evaluator_agrees === true` → green "Agree" badge with testid `inspector-agree`
     - `evaluator_agrees === false` → red "Disagree" badge with testid `inspector-disagree`
     - `evaluator_agrees === null` → gray "Pending" badge with testid `inspector-agree-pending`
   - Render the AgreementBadge in the sentence-detail header inside the Sheet, alongside drop_reason.

7. `web/app/generation/components/verified_report_view.tsx`
   - Add report header badges showing `report.generator_model`, `report.evaluator_model`, and `family_segregation_passed` indicator (testid `family-segregated`).

8. `web/app/sentence_hover_test/_demo.tsx`
   - Add `evaluator_model: "strict_verify_v1"`, `family_segregation_passed: true` to demo VerifiedReport.
   - 3 kept synthetic sentences exercising all 3 badge states without needing `show_dropped`:
     - sentence A: `verifier_pass:true / evaluator_agrees:true` → Agree badge.
     - sentence B: `verifier_pass:true / evaluator_agrees:false` → Disagree badge (real future-state when LLM judge disagrees with rule-based pass).
     - sentence C: `verifier_pass:true / evaluator_agrees:null` → Pending badge.

9. `web/tests/e2e/sentence_inspector_agreement.spec.ts` (new)
   - Test 1: click sentence A → assert `inspector-agree` visible.
   - Test 2: click sentence B → assert `inspector-disagree` visible (per Codex iter 2 P2).
   - Test 3: click sentence C → assert `inspector-agree-pending` visible.
   - Test 4: assert `family-segregated` badge visible in header.

## Risks for Codex Red-Team
1. **Backward compat:** `evaluator_model` is a NEW required field on `VerifiedReport`. All existing fixtures (~6 test files) need updating in same diff — risk of missed fixture → test failure. Audit + update systematically.
2. **Validator semantics:** `evaluator_agrees=True` + `verifier_pass=False` is forbidden. But `evaluator_agrees=False` + `verifier_pass=True` (rule-based said pass, LLM judge said fail) is ALLOWED — represents the real disagreement signal a future two-family judge surfaces.
3. **CHARTER §1 LOC cap:** estimated ~120 LOC net; under 200.
4. **§9.4 N/A frontend.**
5. **Honest substrate:** today's `evaluator_agrees=verifier_pass` is rule-based-only; field is meaningful when real LLM judge wires in (separate Issue). Brief is explicit about this.

## Acceptance criteria

1. `VerifiedReport` schema has `evaluator_model` (required str), `family_segregation_passed` (bool, default True).
2. `VerifiedSentence` has `evaluator_agrees: bool | None` with validator forbidding `True + verifier_pass=False`.
3. Generator orchestrator populates the new fields with rule-based defaults.
4. Frontend types match.
5. Inspector renders 3 badge states (Agree/Disagree/Pending) with testids.
6. Header shows generator/evaluator model names + family-segregation badge.
7. Demo fixture exercises all 3 agreement states.
8. Playwright covers happy + pending + family-segregated header.
9. All existing pytest fixtures updated to pass new required field.
10. CHARTER §1 LOC cap respected (≤200 net).

**Forced enumeration:** before verdict, write one line per criterion 1-10.

**Completeness check:** list files actually read.

  45:     verify_sentence_to_record,
  46: )
  47: from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import (
  48:     GenerationError,
  49:     Section,
  50:     VerifiedReport,
  51:     VerifiedSentence,
  52: )
  53: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  54: 
  55: 
  56: DEFAULT_VERIFIER_PASS_THRESHOLD = 0.40
  57: DEFAULT_GENERATOR_MODEL_LABEL = "stub-generator"
  58: 
  59: 
  60: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  61: # completion_fn protocol
  62: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  63: 
  64: class GeneratorCompletionFn(Protocol):
  65:     """LLM adapter contract.
  66: 
  67:     Given a prompt + section context, return raw generated text. The
  68:     orchestrator parses the returned text into sentences and runs each
  69:     through strict_verify. Implementations must be deterministic-given-
  70:     input enough to be testable.
  71:     """
  72: 
  73:     def __call__(
  74:         self,
  75:         prompt: str,
  76:         section_plan: SectionPlan,
  77:         pool: EvidencePool,
  78:     ) -> str: ...
  79: 
  80: 
  81: def _default_completion_fn(
  82:     prompt: str,
  83:     section_plan: SectionPlan,
  84:     pool: EvidencePool,
  85: ) -> str:
  86:     """Sentinel — refuses to run.
  87: 
  88:     PR 6 ships orchestrator with NO real LLM adapter. Callers MUST inject
  89:     one. PR 7 will ship the real OpenRouter completion_fn.
  90:     """
  91:     raise NotImplementedError(
  92:         "no completion_fn injected. slice 003 PR 7 ships the real "
  93:         "OpenRouter-backed generator; for unit tests inject a stub."
  94:     )
  95: 
  96: 
  97: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  98: # Sentence splitter (simple — replace with spaCy if needed)
  99: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 100: 
 101: # Split on sentence-ending punctuation followed by whitespace + capital
 102: # letter or end-of-string. Conservative; preserves provenance tokens.
 103: _SENTENCE_SPLIT_RE = re.compile(r"(?<=[.!?])\s+(?=[A-Z\[])")
 104: 
 105: 
 106: def _split_sentences(text: str) -> list[str]:
 107:     """Split `text` into sentences. Strips empty/whitespace-only entries."""
 108:     raw = _SENTENCE_SPLIT_RE.split(text.strip())
 109:     return [s.strip() for s in raw if s.strip()]
 110: 
 111: 
 112: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 113: # Validation
 114: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 115: 
 116: def _validate_pool(pool: EvidencePool) -> GenerationError | None:
 117:     if not pool.adequacy.is_adequate:
 118:         return GenerationError(
 119:             code="inadequate_pool",
 120:             message=(
 121:                 f"pool {pool.pool_id} adequacy.is_adequate=False; "
 122:                 f"reason: {pool.adequacy.failure_reason}"
 123:             ),
 124:             pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 125:             decision_id=pool.decision_id,
 126:         )
 127:     return None
 128: 
 129: 
 130: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 131: # Per-section generation + verification
 132: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 133: 
 134: def _generate_and_verify_section(
 135:     section_plan: SectionPlan,
 136:     pool: EvidencePool,
 137:     completion_fn: GeneratorCompletionFn,
 138:     threshold: float,
 139: ) -> Section:
 140:     """Run completion_fn for one section, verify each sentence,
 141:     regenerate ONCE if pass-rate is below threshold."""
 142: 
 143:     def attempt() -> tuple[list[VerifiedSentence], float]:
 144:         raw = completion_fn(
 145:             prompt=section_plan.section_brief,
 146:             section_plan=section_plan,
 147:             pool=pool,
 148:         )
 149:         sentences = _split_sentences(raw)
 150:         records = [
 151:             verify_sentence_to_record(s, section_plan.section_id, pool)
 152:             for s in sentences
 153:         ]
 154:         return records, section_pass_rate(records)
 155: 
 156:     records, rate = attempt()
 157:     status = "verified"
 158: 
 159:     if rate < threshold:
 160:         records2, rate2 = attempt()
 161:         if rate2 >= threshold:
 162:             records = records2
 163:             rate = rate2
 164:             status = "regenerated"
 165:         else:
 166:             # Both attempts failed — mark dropped + keep the better attempt
 167:             # so audit bundle shows what was tried.
 168:             if rate2 > rate:
 169:                 records, rate = records2, rate2
 170:             status = "dropped"
 171: 
 172:     return Section(
 173:         section_id=section_plan.section_id,
 174:         section_title=section_plan.section_title,
 175:         verified_sentences=records,
 176:         section_verify_pass_rate=rate,
 177:         section_status=status,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
 178:     )
 179: 
 180: 
 181: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 182: # Public orchestrator
 183: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 184: 
 185: def process_generation(
 186:     pool: EvidencePool,
 187:     completion_fn: GeneratorCompletionFn = _default_completion_fn,
 188:     blueprint: Blueprint | None = None,
 189:     verifier_pass_threshold: float = DEFAULT_VERIFIER_PASS_THRESHOLD,
 190:     scope_class: str | None = None,
 191:     generator_model: str = DEFAULT_GENERATOR_MODEL_LABEL,
 192: ) -> VerifiedReport | GenerationError:
 193:     """Run an EvidencePool through generator + strict-verify.
 194: 
 195:     Returns:
 196:         VerifiedReport on either success path or all-sections-dropped abort.
 197:         GenerationError when input pool is structurally invalid OR
 198:             completion_fn is the sentinel default OR raises persistently.
 199:     """
 200:     err = _validate_pool(pool)
 201:     if err is not None:
 202:         return err
 203: 
 204:     started = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
 205:     t_start = time.perf_counter()
 206: 
 207:     if blueprint is None:
 208:         # scope_class is preferred; falls back to DEFAULT_BLUEPRINT (efficacy)
 209:         # when None. EvidencePool does not currently carry scope_class —
 210:         # callers (e.g. the FastAPI route) must thread it through from the
 211:         # ScopeDecision that triggered retrieval.
 212:         blueprint = blueprint_for_scope_class(scope_class)
 213: 
 214:     # Derive a real generator_model label when the injected completion_fn
 215:     # exposes one (e.g. RealCompletion.model_label). Stub functions used
 216:     # in tests don't have it, so we fall back to the explicit arg.
 217:     effective_model = generator_model
 218:     if generator_model == DEFAULT_GENERATOR_MODEL_LABEL:
 219:         candidate = getattr(completion_fn, "model_label", None)
 220:         if isinstance(candidate, str) and candidate.strip():
 221:             effective_model = candidate
 222: 
 223:     # Generate all sections in parallel. Each section calls the LLM 1-2
 224:     # times (regen on threshold-fail). With 4 sections, parallel reduces
 225:     # latency from ~4-8 LLM calls serial to ~1-2 LLM calls wall-clock.
 226:     sections_by_idx: dict[int, Section] = {}
 227:     fatal_error: GenerationError | None = None
 228: 
 229:     with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=len(blueprint.sections)) as pool_exec:
 230:         future_to_idx = {
 231:             pool_exec.submit(
 232:                 _generate_and_verify_section,
 233:                 plan,
 234:                 pool,
 235:                 completion_fn,
 236:                 verifier_pass_threshold,
 237:             ): idx
 238:             for idx, plan in enumerate(blueprint.sections)
 239:         }
 240:         for future in as_completed(future_to_idx):
 241:             idx = future_to_idx[future]
 242:             try:
 243:                 sections_by_idx[idx] = future.result()
 244:             except NotImplementedError:
 245:                 fatal_error = GenerationError(
 246:                     code="completion_backend_unavailable",
 247:                     message=(
 248:                         "completion_fn is the sentinel default; inject a real "
 249:                         "fn (PR 7) or test stub"
 250:                     ),
 251:                     pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 252:                     decision_id=pool.decision_id,
 253:                 )
 254:                 break
 255:             except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
 256:                 fatal_error = GenerationError(
 257:                     code="completion_backend_unavailable",
 258:                     message=f"completion_fn raised {type(exc).__name__}: {exc}",
 259:                     pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 260:                     decision_id=pool.decision_id,
 261:                 )
 262:                 break
 263: 
 264:     if fatal_error is not None:
 265:         return fatal_error
 266: 
 267:     # Preserve blueprint section order
 268:     sections: list[Section] = [
 269:         sections_by_idx[i] for i in range(len(blueprint.sections))
 270:     ]
 271: 
 272:     finished = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
 273:     elapsed_ms = int((time.perf_counter() - t_start) * 1000)
 274: 
 275:     # Aggregate pass rate over ALL sentences (kept + dropped) across non-dropped sections.
 276:     kept_sections = [s for s in sections if s.section_status != "dropped"]
 277:     if kept_sections:
 278:         total = sum(len(s.verified_sentences) for s in kept_sections)
 279:         passed = sum(
 280:             sum(1 for v in s.verified_sentences if v.verifier_pass)
 281:             for s in kept_sections
 282:         )
 283:         overall_rate = passed / total if total > 0 else 0.0
 284:         pipeline_verdict = "success"
 285:     else:
 286:         # Every section dropped -> abort. For schema validation, we must
 287:         # carry only dropped sections through.
 288:         sections = [s for s in sections if s.section_status == "dropped"]
 289:         overall_rate = 0.0
 290:         pipeline_verdict = "abort_no_verified_sections"
 291: 
 292:     # When verdict=success, the schema requires sections list to contain
 293:     # only non-dropped OR the verdict consistency check fails. Filter:
 294:     if pipeline_verdict == "success":
 295:         sections = kept_sections
 296: 
 297:     return VerifiedReport(
 298:         pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 299:         decision_id=pool.decision_id,
 300:         sections=sections,
 301:         overall_verify_pass_rate=overall_rate,
 302:         pipeline_verdict=pipeline_verdict,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
 303:         generator_model=effective_model,
 304:         verifier_pass_threshold=verifier_pass_threshold,
 305:         started_at_utc=started,
 306:         finished_at_utc=finished,
 307:         latency_ms=elapsed_ms,
 308:         cost_usd=0.0,
 309:     )

   1: """VerifiedReport schema for slice 003 (generator + strict-verify).
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_003/architecture_proposal.md` §"verified_report.py".
   4: 
   5: Pure-types module. No I/O, no LLM, no network. Slice 003's
   6: process_generation() consumes an EvidencePool (slice 002 output) and
   7: produces a VerifiedReport, which slice 004 will export as an audit
   8: bundle.
   9: 
  10: Lives in `polaris_graph.generator2` (note the `2`) to keep separation
  11: from heritage `polaris_graph.generator` (multi_section, live_deepseek)
  12: which serves the legacy honest-rebuild pipeline. Coexistence by design
  13: per PLAN.md §4 Heritage Import.
  14: """
  15: 
  16: from __future__ import annotations
  17: 
  18: import uuid
  19: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  20: from typing import Literal
  21: 
  22: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, field_validator, model_validator
  23: 
  24: 
  25: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  26: # Type literals
  27: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  28: 
  29: SectionStatus = Literal["verified", "regenerated", "dropped"]
  30: """Per-section outcome from strict_verify:
  31: 
  32: - "verified": original generation passed >=verifier_pass_threshold of
  33:   sentences strict-verified
  34: - "regenerated": original failed; regeneration attempt passed
  35: - "dropped": both attempts failed; section excluded from final report
  36: """
  37: 
  38: PipelineVerdict = Literal["success", "abort_no_verified_sections"]
  39: """Top-level verdict per CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 4."""
  40: 
  41: DropReason = Literal[
  42:     "invalid_token",       # token doesn't reference a known source_id
  43:     "span_out_of_range",   # span_start > span_end or > len(full_text)
  44:     "numeric_mismatch",    # decimal in sentence not present in cited span
  45:     "overlap_too_low",     # < min_content_overlap shared content words
  46:     "no_provenance_token", # sentence has no [#ev:...:start-end] tokens
  47: ]
  48: 
  49: 
  50: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  51: # VerifiedSentence — atomic verified unit
  52: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  53: 
  54: class VerifiedSentence(BaseModel):
  55:     """A single sentence emitted by the generator after strict-verify.
  56: 
  57:     Sentences that fail strict_verify are still represented here with
  58:     `verifier_pass=False` and a `drop_reason`, so the audit bundle can
  59:     surface "what got proposed and dropped" alongside "what shipped."
  60:     """
  61: 
  62:     section_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
  63:     sentence_text: str = Field(min_length=1)
  64:     provenance_tokens: list[str] = Field(
  65:         default_factory=list,
  66:         description="Token strings of form '[#ev:<source_id>:<start>-<end>]'",
  67:     )
  68:     verifier_pass: bool
  69:     drop_reason: DropReason | None = None
  70: 
  71:     @model_validator(mode="after")
  72:     def _drop_reason_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedSentence":
  73:         if self.verifier_pass is False and self.drop_reason is None:
  74:             raise ValueError(
  75:                 "drop_reason is required when verifier_pass=False"
  76:             )
  77:         if self.verifier_pass is True and self.drop_reason is not None:
  78:             raise ValueError(
  79:                 "drop_reason must be None when verifier_pass=True"
  80:             )
  81:         return self
  82: 
  83: 
  84: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  85: # Section
  86: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  87: 
  88: class Section(BaseModel):
  89:     """A report section (e.g. 'Population', 'Outcomes').
  90: 
  91:     `verified_sentences` includes both passed AND dropped sentences for
  92:     audit completeness; UI filters by `verifier_pass` when rendering the
  93:     user-facing report. `section_verify_pass_rate` is over all attempted
  94:     sentences (not just kept ones).
  95:     """
  96: 
  97:     section_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
  98:     section_title: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
  99:     verified_sentences: list[VerifiedSentence] = Field(default_factory=list)
 100:     section_verify_pass_rate: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
 101:     section_status: SectionStatus
 102: 
 103:     def kept_sentences(self) -> list[VerifiedSentence]:
 104:         """Filter to sentences that passed strict_verify."""
 105:         return [s for s in self.verified_sentences if s.verifier_pass]
 106: 
 107: 
 108: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 109: # VerifiedReport
 110: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 111: 
 112: class VerifiedReport(BaseModel):
 113:     """The slice 003 output. Bound to a slice-002 pool via pool_id +
 114:     a slice-001 decision via decision_id. Same pool can produce different
 115:     reports across runs (LLM nondeterminism); report_id distinguishes them.
 116:     """
 117: 
 118:     report_id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
 119:     pool_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
 120:     decision_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
 121:     sections: list[Section] = Field(default_factory=list)
 122:     overall_verify_pass_rate: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
 123:     pipeline_verdict: PipelineVerdict
 124:     generator_model: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
 125:     verifier_pass_threshold: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
 126:     started_at_utc: datetime
 127:     finished_at_utc: datetime
 128:     latency_ms: int = Field(ge=0)
 129:     cost_usd: float = Field(ge=0.0)
 130: 
 131:     @field_validator("finished_at_utc")
 132:     @classmethod
 133:     def _finished_after_started(cls, v: datetime, info) -> datetime:
 134:         started = info.data.get("started_at_utc")
 135:         if started is not None and v < started:
 136:             raise ValueError(
 137:                 "finished_at_utc must be >= started_at_utc"
 138:             )
 139:         return v
 140: 
 141:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 142:     def _verdict_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedReport":
 143:         """If verdict=success, at least one section must be verified or
 144:         regenerated. If verdict=abort_no_verified_sections, every section
 145:         (if any) must be 'dropped' or sections may be empty."""
 146:         if self.pipeline_verdict == "success":
 147:             kept = [
 148:                 s for s in self.sections if s.section_status != "dropped"
 149:             ]
 150:             if not kept:
 151:                 raise ValueError(
 152:                     "pipeline_verdict='success' requires at least one "
 153:                     "non-dropped section"
 154:                 )
 155:         else:  # abort_no_verified_sections
 156:             for section in self.sections:
 157:                 if section.section_status != "dropped":
 158:                     raise ValueError(
 159:                         "pipeline_verdict='abort_no_verified_sections' "
 160:                         "requires all sections (if any) to be dropped"
 161:                     )
 162:         return self
 163: 
 164:     def kept_sections(self) -> list[Section]:
 165:         """Filter to non-dropped sections."""
 166:         return [s for s in self.sections if s.section_status != "dropped"]

 succeeded in 3131ms:
   1: """Strict verifier per CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 3.
   2: 
   3: Per-sentence check enforcing:
   4:   (a) at least one provenance token present
   5:   (b) every token references an evidence_id in the pool
   6:   (c) span bounds are valid (0 <= start <= end <= len(text))
   7:   (d) every decimal in the sentence appears in the cited spans
   8:   (e) sentence and span share >= MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP content words
   9: 
  10: Returns a (verifier_pass: bool, drop_reason: str | None) pair, or directly
  11: constructs a VerifiedSentence for use by the generator orchestrator.
  12: 
  13: Pure-functions module: no I/O, no LLM, no network.
  14: 
  15: Tunables (read at call time so tests can override):
  16:   PG_PROVENANCE_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP — minimum shared content words (default 2)
  17: """
  18: 
  19: from __future__ import annotations
  20: 
  21: import os
  22: import re
  23: 
  24: from polaris_graph.generator2.provenance import (
  25:     ProvenanceToken,
  26:     extract_tokens,
  27:     get_span_text,
  28:     strip_tokens,
  29:     validate_token_against_pool,
  30: )
  31: from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import (
  32:     DropReason,
  33:     VerifiedSentence,
  34: )
  35: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  36: 
  37: 
  38: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  39: # Tunables
  40: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  41: 
  42: DEFAULT_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP = 2
  43: 
  44: # Minimal English stopword list. Strict-verify's content-word overlap should
  45: # count substantive vocabulary, not function words. This is intentionally
  46: # small — the rule is conservative ("at least 2 shared content words")
  47: # so even a short stoplist yields the right behavior.
  48: _STOPWORDS: frozenset[str] = frozenset({
  49:     "a", "an", "the", "and", "or", "but", "if", "of", "in", "on", "at",
  50:     "to", "for", "with", "as", "by", "from", "into", "through", "during",
  51:     "before", "after", "above", "below", "between", "is", "are", "was",
  52:     "were", "be", "been", "being", "have", "has", "had", "having", "do",
  53:     "does", "did", "doing", "will", "would", "should", "could", "may",
  54:     "might", "must", "can", "this", "that", "these", "those", "it",
  55:     "its", "their", "there", "they", "them", "we", "us", "our", "you",
  56:     "your", "i", "me", "my", "he", "she", "his", "her",
  57: })
  58: 
  59: _DECIMAL_RE = re.compile(r"\d+(?:\.\d+)?")
  60: _WORD_RE = re.compile(r"[A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9_\-]+")
  61: 
  62: 
  63: def _min_overlap_threshold() -> int:
  64:     raw = os.environ.get("PG_PROVENANCE_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP", "")
  65:     try:
  66:         return max(0, int(raw))
  67:     except ValueError:
  68:         return DEFAULT_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP
  69: 
  70: 
  71: def _content_words(text: str) -> set[str]:
  72:     """Lowercase content words (>=3 chars, not stopwords) from `text`."""
  73:     return {
  74:         m.group(0).lower()
  75:         for m in _WORD_RE.finditer(text)
  76:         if len(m.group(0)) >= 3 and m.group(0).lower() not in _STOPWORDS
  77:     }
  78: 
  79: 
  80: def _decimals(text: str) -> set[str]:
  81:     """Numeric tokens (integers + decimals) from `text`."""
  82:     return {m.group(0) for m in _DECIMAL_RE.finditer(text)}
  83: 
  84: 
  85: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  86: # Per-sentence verifier
  87: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  88: 
  89: def verify_sentence(
  90:     sentence_text: str,
  91:     pool: EvidencePool,
  92:     min_content_overlap: int | None = None,
  93: ) -> tuple[bool, DropReason | None]:
  94:     """Return (verifier_pass, drop_reason) for `sentence_text` against `pool`.
  95: 
  96:     Pass: returns (True, None).
  97:     Fail: returns (False, drop_reason) with reason from DropReason literal.
  98: 
  99:     Implements CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 3 in order:
 100:       1. at least one well-formed token        → no_provenance_token
 101:       2. every token references known source_id → invalid_token
 102:       3. spans within source bounds            → span_out_of_range
 103:       4. every decimal in sentence in spans    → numeric_mismatch
 104:       5. >=N shared content words              → overlap_too_low
 105:     """
 106:     threshold = (
 107:         min_content_overlap
 108:         if min_content_overlap is not None
 109:         else _min_overlap_threshold()
 110:     )
 111: 
 112:     tokens = extract_tokens(sentence_text)
 113:     if not tokens:
 114:         return False, "no_provenance_token"
 115: 
 116:     # Validate each token against the pool. Collect span texts for
 117:     # later numeric + overlap checks.
 118:     span_texts: list[str] = []
 119:     for token in tokens:
 120:         reason = validate_token_against_pool(token, pool)
 121:         if reason == "invalid_token":
 122:             return False, "invalid_token"
 123:         if reason == "span_out_of_range":
 124:             return False, "span_out_of_range"
 125:         # Token valid — fetch its span text
 126:         span = get_span_text(token, pool)
 127:         if span is None:
 128:             # Belt-and-suspenders: token validated but get_span_text said no.
 129:             return False, "span_out_of_range"
 130:         span_texts.append(span)
 131: 
 132:     sentence_clean = strip_tokens(sentence_text)
 133:     combined_span = " ".join(span_texts)
 134: 
 135:     # Decimal match: every decimal in sentence must appear in the combined
 136:     # span text. Permits the spans to contain MORE decimals than the
 137:     # sentence cites — that's fine; the constraint is one-way.
 138:     sentence_decimals = _decimals(sentence_clean)
 139:     span_decimals = _decimals(combined_span)
 140:     if not sentence_decimals.issubset(span_decimals):
 141:         return False, "numeric_mismatch"
 142: 
 143:     # Content-word overlap
 144:     sentence_words = _content_words(sentence_clean)
 145:     span_words = _content_words(combined_span)
 146:     overlap = len(sentence_words & span_words)
 147:     if overlap < threshold:
 148:         return False, "overlap_too_low"
 149: 
 150:     return True, None
 151: 
 152: 
 153: def verify_sentence_to_record(
 154:     sentence_text: str,
 155:     section_id: str,
 156:     pool: EvidencePool,
 157:     min_content_overlap: int | None = None,
 158: ) -> VerifiedSentence:
 159:     """Convenience: wrap verify_sentence into a VerifiedSentence record.
 160: 
 161:     Used by the generator orchestrator to build Section.verified_sentences.
 162:     """
 163:     passed, reason = verify_sentence(
 164:         sentence_text, pool, min_content_overlap=min_content_overlap
 165:     )
 166:     tokens = [t.raw for t in extract_tokens(sentence_text)]
 167:     return VerifiedSentence(
 168:         section_id=section_id,
 169:         sentence_text=sentence_text,
 170:         provenance_tokens=tokens,
 171:         verifier_pass=passed,
 172:         drop_reason=reason,
 173:     )
 174: 
 175: 
 176: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 177: # Section-level rollup
 178: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 179: 
 180: def section_pass_rate(sentences: list[VerifiedSentence]) -> float:
 181:     """Fraction of sentences that passed verify, in [0.0, 1.0].
 182: 
 183:     Empty list returns 0.0 (vacuously below any threshold).
 184:     """
 185:     if not sentences:
 186:         return 0.0
 187:     passed = sum(1 for s in sentences if s.verifier_pass)
 188:     return passed / len(sentences)

 196:           <CardTitle className="text-lg">Verified report</CardTitle>
 197:           <VerdictBadge verdict={report.pipeline_verdict} />
 198:         </CardHeader>
 199:         <CardContent>
 200:           <dl className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-x-6 gap-y-1 text-sm">
 201:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground">Generator</dt>
 202:             <dd className="text-foreground font-medium">
 203:               {report.generator_model}
 204:             </dd>
 205:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground">Pass rate</dt>
 206:             <dd className="text-foreground font-medium">
 207:               {Math.round(report.overall_verify_pass_rate * 100)}%
 208:             </dd>
 209:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground">Sections</dt>
 210:             <dd className="text-foreground font-medium">
 211:               {
 212:                 report.sections.filter((s) => s.section_status !== "dropped")
 213:                   .length
 214:               }{" "}
 215:               kept ·{" "}
 216:               {
 217:                 report.sections.filter((s) => s.section_status === "dropped")
 218:                   .length
 219:               }{" "}
 220:               dropped
 221:             </dd>
 222:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground">Latency</dt>
 223:             <dd className="text-foreground font-medium">
 224:               {report.latency_ms} ms
 225:             </dd>
 226:           </dl>
 227:         </CardContent>
 228:       </Card>
 229: 
 230:       {report.sections.map((section) => (
 231:         <SectionCard
 232:           key={section.section_id}
 233:           section={section}
 234:           show_dropped={show_dropped}
 235:           hovered_id={hovered_id}
 236:           onSelect={(id, sentence) => setInspector({ id, sentence })}
 237:         />
 238:       ))}
 239:       <SentenceInspector
 240:         open={inspector !== null}
 241:         onOpenChange={(open) => {
 242:           if (!open) setInspector(null);
 243:         }}
 244:         sentence={inspector?.sentence ?? null}
 245:         sentence_id={inspector?.id ?? null}
 246:         pool={pool}
 247:       />
 248:     </div>
 249:   );
 250: }

  50:   status: number;
  51:   body: unknown;

  54: async function asJsonOrThrow<T>(response: Response): Promise<T> {
  55:   const body = await response.json().catch(() => null);
  56:   if (!response.ok) {
  57:     const error = new Error(
  58:       `POLARIS backend returned ${response.status}`,
  59:     ) as ApiError;
  60:     error.status = response.status;
  61:     error.body = body;
  62:     throw error;
  63:   }
  64:   return body as T;
  65: }

 285: export function downloadBundleAsJson(bundle: EvidenceContract): void {
 286:   const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(bundle, null, 2)], {
 287:     type: "application/json",
 288:   });
 289:   const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
 290:   const link = document.createElement("a");
 291:   link.href = url;
 292:   link.download = `polaris_bundle_${bundle.run_id}.json`;
 293:   document.body.appendChild(link);
 294:   link.click();
 295:   document.body.removeChild(link);
 296:   URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
 297: }

 299: export interface StreamEvent {
 300:   event: string;
 301:   data: Record<string, unknown>;
 302: }
 303: 
 304: /**
 305:  * Subscribe to /stream/{runId}. Returns the EventSource so the caller can
 306:  * close it. Per Phase 0 stub, the backend yields 5 deterministic events.
 307:  */
 308: export function subscribeToRun(
 309:   runId: string,
 310:   onEvent: (event: StreamEvent) => void,
 311:   onError?: (error: Event) => void,
 312: ): EventSource {
 313:   const source = new EventSource(`${BACKEND_URL}/stream/${runId}`);
 314: 
 315:   const handler = (event: MessageEvent<string>) => {
 316:     try {
 317:       const parsed = JSON.parse(event.data);
 318:       onEvent({ event: event.type, data: parsed });
 319:     } catch {
 320:       onEvent({ event: event.type, data: { raw: event.data } });
 321:     }
 322:   };
 323: 
 324:   for (const eventName of [
 325:     "scope_decision",
 326:     "retrieval_progress",
 327:     "verifier_verdict",
 328:     "section_complete",
 329:     "run_complete",
 330:   ]) {
 331:     source.addEventListener(eventName, handler);
 332:   }
 333: 
 334:   if (onError) {
 335:     source.onerror = onError;
 336:   }
 337:   return source;
 338: }

 427: export async function runIntake(
 428:   question: string,
 429: ): Promise<IntakeSuccessResponse> {
 430:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/intake`, {
 431:     method: "POST",
 432:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 433:     body: JSON.stringify({ question }),
 434:   });
 435: 
 436:   if (response.status === 400) {
 437:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 438:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as IntakeErrorBody | null;
 439:     if (body && body.error) {
 440:       throw new IntakeBadRequestError(body);
 441:     }
 442:   }
 443: 
 444:   return asJsonOrThrow<IntakeSuccessResponse>(response);
 445: }

 524: export async function runRetrieval(
 525:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision,
 526: ): Promise<RetrievalSuccessResponse> {
 527:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/retrieval`, {
 528:     method: "POST",
 529:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 530:     body: JSON.stringify({ decision }),
 531:   });
 532: 
 533:   if (response.status === 400) {
 534:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 535:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as RetrievalErrorBody | null;
 536:     if (body && body.error) {

 556: /** Convenience: count sources matching a given tier. */
 557: export function countSourcesByTier(
 558:   pool: EvidencePool,
 559:   tier: RetrievalSourceTier,
 560: ): number {
 561:   return pool.sources.filter((s) => s.tier === tier).length;
 562: }
 563: 
 564: /** Convenience: dedupe + sort sources by tier (T1 first), then by domain. */
 565: export function sortSourcesByTier(
 566:   sources: RetrievalSource[],
 567: ): RetrievalSource[] {
 568:   const tier_rank: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, number> = {
 569:     T1: 0,
 570:     T2: 1,
 571:     T3: 2,
 572:   };
 573:   return [...sources].sort((a, b) => {
 574:     const t = tier_rank[a.tier] - tier_rank[b.tier];
 575:     if (t !== 0) return t;
 576:     return a.domain.localeCompare(b.domain);
 577:   });
 578: }

 644: 
 645: export class GenerationBadRequestError extends Error {
 646:   code: GenerationErrorBody["code"];
 647:   pool_id: string | null;
 648:   decision_id: string | null;
 649:   constructor(body: GenerationErrorBody) {
 650:     super(body.message);
 651:     this.name = "GenerationBadRequestError";
 652:     this.code = body.code;
 653:     this.pool_id = body.pool_id;
 654:     this.decision_id = body.decision_id;
 655:   }
 656: }
 657: 
 658: export async function runGeneration(
 659:   pool: EvidencePool,
 660:   scope_class?: string | null,
 661: ): Promise<GenerationSuccessResponse> {
 662:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/generation`, {
 663:     method: "POST",
 664:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 665:     body: JSON.stringify({ pool, scope_class: scope_class ?? null }),
 666:   });
 667: 
 668:   if (response.status === 400) {
 669:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 670:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as GenerationErrorBody | null;
 671:     if (body && body.error) {
 672:       throw new GenerationBadRequestError(body);
 673:     }
 674:   }
 675: 
 676:   return asJsonOrThrow<GenerationSuccessResponse>(response);
 677: }

 703: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

 705: // Mirrors src/polaris_graph/api/audit_bundle_route.py.

 707: 
 708: export interface AuditBundleErrorBody {
 709:   error: true;
 710:   code:
 711:     | "fk_chain_mismatch"
 712:     | "verdict_not_success"
 713:     | "cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot"
 714:     | "copyrighted_span_in_bundle"
 715:     | "gpg_unavailable"
 716:     | "sign_failed";
 717:   message: string;
 718:   report_id: string | null;
 719: }
 720: 
 721: export class AuditBundleError extends Error {
 722:   code: AuditBundleErrorBody["code"];
 723:   report_id: string | null;
 724:   constructor(body: AuditBundleErrorBody) {
 725:     super(body.message);
 726:     this.name = "AuditBundleError";
 727:     this.code = body.code;
 728:     this.report_id = body.report_id;
 729:   }
 730: }
 731: 
 732: /**
 733:  * Build + download a GPG-signed audit bundle for the given BPEI chain.
 734:  *
 735:  * Returns a Blob of the audit_<id>.tar.gz on success. On HTTP 4xx/5xx
 736:  * with a structured error body, throws AuditBundleError with the .code
 737:  * field set so callers can show specific UX (e.g. "GPG signer not
 738:  * configured" vs "report verdict not success").
 739:  */
 740: export async function downloadAuditBundle(
 741:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision,
 742:   pool: EvidencePool,
 743:   report: VerifiedReport,
 744: ): Promise<Blob> {
 745:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/audit-bundle`, {
 746:     method: "POST",
 747:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 748:     body: JSON.stringify({ decision, pool, report }),
 749:   });
 750:   if (!response.ok) {
 751:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 752:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as AuditBundleErrorBody | null;
 753:     if (body && body.error) {
 754:       throw new AuditBundleError(body);
 755:     }
 756:     throw new Error(`Audit bundle request failed: HTTP ${response.status}`);
 757:   }
 758:   return await response.blob();
 759: }

 784:   });
 785:   if (!response.ok) {

 788:     if (body && body.error) {
 789:       throw new AuditBundleError(body);
 790:     }
 791:     throw new Error(`Bundle preview request failed: HTTP ${response.status}`);

 171: def _success_report(**overrides) -> VerifiedReport:
 172:     started = _now()
 173:     finished = started + timedelta(seconds=10)
 174:     base = dict(
 175:         pool_id="pool-1",
 176:         decision_id="dec-1",
 177:         sections=[
 178:             Section(
 179:                 section_id="sec_population",
 180:                 section_title="Population",
 181:                 verified_sentences=[_kept(), _kept()],
 182:                 section_verify_pass_rate=1.0,
 183:                 section_status="verified",
 184:             )
 185:         ],
 186:         overall_verify_pass_rate=1.0,
 187:         pipeline_verdict="success",
 188:         generator_model="deepseek-v4-flash",
 189:         verifier_pass_threshold=0.4,
 190:         started_at_utc=started,
 191:         finished_at_utc=finished,
 192:         latency_ms=10000,
 193:         cost_usd=0.05,
 194:     )
 195:     base.update(overrides)
 196:     return VerifiedReport(**base)  # type: ignore[arg-type]

 157: def test_slice_005_golden(golden_path: Path | None):
 158:     if golden_path is None:
 159:         pytest.skip("no goldens")
 160: 
 161:     spec = json.loads(golden_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 162: 
 163:     config = BenchmarkConfig.model_validate(spec["config"])
 164:     polaris_results = {
 165:         qid: _polaris_from_spec(qid, qspec)
 166:         for qid, qspec in spec.get("polaris_results", {}).items()
 167:     }
 168:     chatgpt = spec.get("chatgpt_outputs", {})
 169:     gemini = spec.get("gemini_outputs", {})
 170: 
 171:     sb = run_benchmark(
 172:         config=config,
 173:         polaris_results=polaris_results,
 174:         chatgpt_outputs=chatgpt,
 175:         gemini_outputs=gemini,
 176:     )
 177: 
 178:     expected = spec["expected"]
 179:     assert expected["kind"] == "Scoreboard"
 180: 
 181:     if "polaris_wins_min" in expected:
 182:         assert sb.polaris_wins >= expected["polaris_wins_min"]
 183:     if "external_wins" in expected:
 184:         assert sb.external_wins == expected["external_wins"]
 185:     if "ties" in expected:
 186:         assert sb.ties == expected["ties"]
 187: 
 188:     if "verify_polaris_auto_one" in expected:
 189:         for dim in expected["verify_polaris_auto_one"]:
 190:             for q in sb.per_question:
 191:                 p_score = q.polaris.by_dimension.get(dim)
 192:                 assert p_score == 1.0, (
 193:                     f"{golden_path.name}: polaris {dim} should be 1.0 "
 194:                     f"for {q.question_id}, got {p_score}"
 195:                 )
 196: 
 197:     if "polaris_refusal_score" in expected:
 198:         for q in sb.per_question:
 199:             p = q.polaris.by_dimension["refusal_correctness"]
 200:             assert p == expected["polaris_refusal_score"]
 201:     if "chatgpt_refusal_score" in expected:
 202:         for q in sb.per_question:
 203:             c = q.chatgpt.by_dimension["refusal_correctness"]
 204:             assert c == expected["chatgpt_refusal_score"]
 205:     if "gemini_refusal_score" in expected:
 206:         for q in sb.per_question:
 207:             g = q.gemini.by_dimension["refusal_correctness"]
 208:             assert g == expected["gemini_refusal_score"]
 209: 
 210:     if expected.get("polaris_wins_for_refusal"):
 211:         # POLARIS should beat ChatGPT (1.0 vs 0.0) and tie/beat Gemini
 212:         for q in sb.per_question:
 213:             p = q.polaris.by_dimension["refusal_correctness"]
 214:             c = q.chatgpt.by_dimension["refusal_correctness"]
 215:             assert p > c
 216: 
 217:     if expected.get("chatgpt_has_some_real_scores"):
 218:         for q in sb.per_question:
 219:             populated = [
 220:                 v for v in q.chatgpt.by_dimension.values() if v is not None
 221:             ]
 222:             assert len(populated) > 0
 223: 
 224:     if expected.get("gemini_all_external_dims_none_or_zero"):
 225:         for q in sb.per_question:
 226:             for dim in ALL_DIMENSIONS:
 227:                 v = q.gemini.by_dimension.get(dim)
 228:                 # When external text missing, most dims return None except
 229:                 # for refusal_correctness on bait + auditability/latency
 230:                 # which return defaults. Enforce: nothing > 0.0.
 231:                 if v is not None:
 232:                     assert v <= 1.0

 succeeded in 1585ms:
   1: """BEAT-BOTH scorer orchestrator — wires runner + loader + dimension scorers.
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_005/architecture_proposal.md` §"beat_both_scorer".
   4: 
   5: For each BenchmarkQuestion, runs all 7 dimension scorers against
   6: (polaris_result, chatgpt_text, gemini_text) and assembles a Scoreboard
   7: that aggregates per-system per-dimension scores.
   8: 
   9: The Scoreboard is the artifact that report_renderer turns into HTML +
  10: Markdown for the demo.
  11: """
  12: 
  13: from __future__ import annotations
  14: 
  15: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  16: from typing import Any
  17: 
  18: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
  19: 
  20: from polaris_graph.benchmark.benchmark_config import (
  21:     BenchmarkConfig,
  22:     BenchmarkQuestion,
  23: )
  24: from polaris_graph.benchmark.dimension_scorers import (
  25:     ALL_DIMENSIONS,
  26:     DimensionName,
  27:     DimensionScore,
  28:     score_auditability,
  29:     score_coverage_completeness,
  30:     score_latency,
  31:     score_numeric_grounding,
  32:     score_provenance_density,
  33:     score_refusal_correctness,
  34:     score_sourcing_tier_mix,
  35: )
  36: from polaris_graph.benchmark.polaris_runner import PolarisRunResult
  37: 
  38: 
  39: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  40: # Scoreboard schema
  41: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  42: 
  43: class SystemScores(BaseModel):
  44:     """One system's scores for a single question (one row in the scoreboard)."""
  45: 
  46:     system: str  # 'polaris' | 'chatgpt' | 'gemini'
  47:     by_dimension: dict[DimensionName, float | None]
  48:     evidence: dict[DimensionName, list[str]] = Field(default_factory=dict)
  49: 
  50: 
  51: class QuestionScores(BaseModel):
  52:     """All systems' scores for one question."""
  53: 
  54:     question_id: str
  55:     question_text: str
  56:     is_refusal_bait: bool
  57:     polaris: SystemScores
  58:     chatgpt: SystemScores
  59:     gemini: SystemScores
  60: 
  61: 
  62: class AggregateScoreboard(BaseModel):
  63:     """Mean per-dimension per-system across all questions."""
  64: 
  65:     polaris_mean: dict[DimensionName, float | None]
  66:     chatgpt_mean: dict[DimensionName, float | None]
  67:     gemini_mean: dict[DimensionName, float | None]
  68:     n_questions: int
  69: 
  70: 
  71: class Scoreboard(BaseModel):
  72:     """Top-level benchmark output."""
  73: 
  74:     benchmark_id: str
  75:     ran_at_utc: datetime = Field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc))
  76:     per_question: list[QuestionScores]
  77:     aggregate: AggregateScoreboard
  78:     polaris_wins: int          # dimensions where polaris > both externals (per-q)
  79:     external_wins: int          # dimensions where some external > polaris (per-q)
  80:     ties: int                   # dimensions where polaris == max external
  81: 
  82: 
  83: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  84: # Per-question scoring
  85: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  86: 
  87: def _polaris_dimension_scores(
  88:     *,
  89:     polaris: PolarisRunResult,
  90:     question: BenchmarkQuestion,
  91: ) -> dict[DimensionName, DimensionScore]:
  92:     """Run all 7 scorers in 'POLARIS-side only' mode (external_text=None)."""
  93:     pool = None
  94:     if polaris.evidence_pool is not None:
  95:         from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  96: 
  97:         pool = EvidencePool.model_validate(polaris.evidence_pool)
  98:     report = None
  99:     if polaris.verified_report is not None:
 100:         from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import VerifiedReport
 101: 
 102:         report = VerifiedReport.model_validate(polaris.verified_report)
 103: 
 104:     scores: dict[DimensionName, DimensionScore] = {}
 105:     scores["sourcing_tier_mix"] = score_sourcing_tier_mix(
 106:         pool=pool, external_text=None, question=question
 107:     )
 108:     scores["numeric_grounding"] = score_numeric_grounding(
 109:         report=report, pool=pool, external_text=None, question=question
 110:     )
 111:     scores["provenance_density"] = score_provenance_density(
 112:         report=report, external_text=None, question=question
 113:     )
 114:     scores["refusal_correctness"] = score_refusal_correctness(
 115:         report=report,
 116:         polaris_intake_status=polaris.intake_status,
 117:         external_text=None,
 118:         question=question,
 119:     )
 120:     scores["coverage_completeness"] = score_coverage_completeness(
 121:         report=report, external_text=None, question=question
 122:     )
 123:     scores["latency"] = score_latency(
 124:         polaris_latency_ms=polaris.total_latency_ms or None,
 125:         external_latency_ms=None,
 126:         question=question,
 127:     )
 128:     scores["auditability"] = score_auditability(
 129:         polaris_bundle_available=polaris.bundle_available,
 130:         external_bundle_available=False,
 131:         question=question,
 132:     )
 133:     return scores
 134: 
 135: 
 136: def _external_dimension_scores(
 137:     *,
 138:     external_text: str | None,
 139:     question: BenchmarkQuestion,
 140: ) -> dict[DimensionName, DimensionScore]:
 141:     """Run all 7 scorers in 'external-side only' mode."""
 142:     scores: dict[DimensionName, DimensionScore] = {}
 143:     scores["sourcing_tier_mix"] = score_sourcing_tier_mix(
 144:         pool=None, external_text=external_text, question=question
 145:     )
 146:     scores["numeric_grounding"] = score_numeric_grounding(
 147:         report=None, pool=None, external_text=external_text, question=question
 148:     )
 149:     scores["provenance_density"] = score_provenance_density(
 150:         report=None, external_text=external_text, question=question
 151:     )
 152:     scores["refusal_correctness"] = score_refusal_correctness(
 153:         report=None,
 154:         polaris_intake_status=None,
 155:         external_text=external_text,
 156:         question=question,
 157:     )
 158:     scores["coverage_completeness"] = score_coverage_completeness(
 159:         report=None, external_text=external_text, question=question
 160:     )
 161:     scores["latency"] = score_latency(
 162:         polaris_latency_ms=None,
 163:         external_latency_ms=None,  # external latencies typically not measured
 164:         question=question,
 165:     )
 166:     scores["auditability"] = score_auditability(
 167:         polaris_bundle_available=False,
 168:         external_bundle_available=False,
 169:         question=question,
 170:     )
 171:     return scores
 172: 
 173: 
 174: def _to_system_scores(
 175:     system: str,
 176:     dim_scores: dict[DimensionName, DimensionScore],
 177:     *,
 178:     use_external: bool,
 179: ) -> SystemScores:
 180:     """Convert dict[dim -> DimensionScore] to flat SystemScores."""
 181:     by_dim: dict[DimensionName, float | None] = {}
 182:     evidence: dict[DimensionName, list[str]] = {}
 183:     for dim, score in dim_scores.items():
 184:         if use_external:
 185:             by_dim[dim] = score.external_score
 186:             evidence[dim] = list(score.external_evidence)
 187:         else:
 188:             by_dim[dim] = score.polaris_score
 189:             evidence[dim] = list(score.polaris_evidence)
 190:     return SystemScores(system=system, by_dimension=by_dim, evidence=evidence)
 191: 
 192: 
 193: def score_question(
 194:     *,
 195:     question: BenchmarkQuestion,
 196:     polaris: PolarisRunResult,
 197:     chatgpt_text: str | None,
 198:     gemini_text: str | None,
 199: ) -> QuestionScores:
 200:     """Score one question across all 3 systems × 7 dimensions."""
 201:     polaris_dim_scores = _polaris_dimension_scores(
 202:         polaris=polaris, question=question
 203:     )
 204:     chatgpt_dim_scores = _external_dimension_scores(
 205:         external_text=chatgpt_text, question=question
 206:     )
 207:     gemini_dim_scores = _external_dimension_scores(
 208:         external_text=gemini_text, question=question
 209:     )
 210: 
 211:     return QuestionScores(
 212:         question_id=question.question_id,
 213:         question_text=question.question_text,
 214:         is_refusal_bait=question.is_refusal_bait,
 215:         polaris=_to_system_scores("polaris", polaris_dim_scores, use_external=False),
 216:         chatgpt=_to_system_scores("chatgpt", chatgpt_dim_scores, use_external=True),
 217:         gemini=_to_system_scores("gemini", gemini_dim_scores, use_external=True),
 218:     )
 219: 
 220: 
 221: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 222: # Aggregation
 223: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 224: 
 225: def _mean_or_none(values: list[float | None]) -> float | None:
 226:     """Mean of non-None values; None when all are None."""
 227:     populated = [v for v in values if v is not None]
 228:     if not populated:
 229:         return None
 230:     return sum(populated) / len(populated)
 231: 
 232: 
 233: def _aggregate(per_question: list[QuestionScores]) -> AggregateScoreboard:
 234:     """Per-system per-dimension means across all questions."""
 235: 
 236:     def _means_for(system_attr: str) -> dict[DimensionName, float | None]:
 237:         out: dict[DimensionName, float | None] = {}
 238:         for dim in ALL_DIMENSIONS:
 239:             values = [
 240:                 getattr(q, system_attr).by_dimension.get(dim)
 241:                 for q in per_question
 242:             ]
 243:             out[dim] = _mean_or_none(values)
 244:         return out
 245: 
 246:     return AggregateScoreboard(
 247:         polaris_mean=_means_for("polaris"),
 248:         chatgpt_mean=_means_for("chatgpt"),
 249:         gemini_mean=_means_for("gemini"),
 250:         n_questions=len(per_question),
 251:     )
 252: 
 253: 
 254: def _count_wins(per_question: list[QuestionScores]) -> tuple[int, int, int]:
 255:     """Per question, per dimension: count polaris vs max(external) outcomes."""
 256:     polaris_wins = 0
 257:     external_wins = 0
 258:     ties = 0
 259:     for q in per_question:
 260:         for dim in ALL_DIMENSIONS:
 261:             p = q.polaris.by_dimension.get(dim)
 262:             c = q.chatgpt.by_dimension.get(dim)
 263:             g = q.gemini.by_dimension.get(dim)
 264:             externals = [v for v in (c, g) if v is not None]
 265:             if p is None and not externals:
 266:                 continue
 267:             if p is None:
 268:                 external_wins += 1
 269:                 continue
 270:             if not externals:
 271:                 polaris_wins += 1
 272:                 continue
 273:             best_external = max(externals)
 274:             if p > best_external:
 275:                 polaris_wins += 1
 276:             elif p < best_external:
 277:                 external_wins += 1
 278:             else:
 279:                 ties += 1
 280:     return polaris_wins, external_wins, ties
 281: 
 282: 
 283: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 284: # Public API
 285: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 286: 
 287: def run_benchmark(
 288:     *,
 289:     config: BenchmarkConfig,
 290:     polaris_results: dict[str, PolarisRunResult],
 291:     chatgpt_outputs: dict[str, str],
 292:     gemini_outputs: dict[str, str],
 293: ) -> Scoreboard:
 294:     """Score every benchmark question across the 3 systems × 7 dimensions."""
 295:     per_question: list[QuestionScores] = []
 296:     for question in config.questions:
 297:         polaris = polaris_results.get(question.question_id)
 298:         if polaris is None:
 299:             polaris = PolarisRunResult(
 300:                 question_id=question.question_id,
 301:                 failure="no PolarisRunResult provided",
 302:             )
 303:         per_question.append(
 304:             score_question(
 305:                 question=question,
 306:                 polaris=polaris,
 307:                 chatgpt_text=chatgpt_outputs.get(question.question_id),
 308:                 gemini_text=gemini_outputs.get(question.question_id),
 309:             )
 310:         )
 311: 
 312:     polaris_wins, external_wins, ties = _count_wins(per_question)
 313: 
 314:     return Scoreboard(
 315:         benchmark_id=config.benchmark_id,
 316:         per_question=per_question,
 317:         aggregate=_aggregate(per_question),
 318:         polaris_wins=polaris_wins,
 319:         external_wins=external_wins,
 320:         ties=ties,
 321:     )

  36: # ---------- Fixtures ----------
  37: 
  38: def _q(
  39:     qid: str = "Q1",
  40:     refusal_bait: bool = False,
  41:     pico: list[str] | None = None,
  42:     keywords: list[str] | None = None,
  43: ) -> BenchmarkQuestion:
  44:     if pico is None:
  45:         pico = ["population", "intervention", "outcome"]
  46:     return BenchmarkQuestion(
  47:         question_id=qid,
  48:         question_text="text",
  49:         scope_class="out_of_scope" if refusal_bait else "clinical_efficacy",
  50:         is_refusal_bait=refusal_bait,
  51:         expected_pico_axes=pico,
  52:         expected_pico_keywords=keywords or [],
  53:     )
  54: 
  55: 
  56: def _src(tier: SourceTier, host: str) -> Source:
  57:     return Source(
  58:         url=f"https://{host}/x",
  59:         domain=host,
  60:         tier=tier,
  61:         title="src",
  62:         snippet="snippet",
  63:         full_text="text" * 30,
  64:         full_text_available=True,
  65:     )
  66: 
  67: 
  68: def _pool(*sources: Source) -> EvidencePool:
  69:     return EvidencePool(
  70:         decision_id="dec",
  71:         sources=list(sources),
  72:         adequacy=AdequacyVerdict(
  73:             is_adequate=True,
  74:             sources_per_tier={
  75:                 SourceTier.T1: sum(1 for s in sources if s.tier == SourceTier.T1),
  76:                 SourceTier.T2: sum(1 for s in sources if s.tier == SourceTier.T2),
  77:                 SourceTier.T3: sum(1 for s in sources if s.tier == SourceTier.T3),
  78:             },
  79:             min_required_per_tier={SourceTier.T1: 0, SourceTier.T2: 0, SourceTier.T3: 0},
  80:         ),
  81:         retrieval_started_at_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
  82:         retrieval_finished_at_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
  83:         latency_ms=0,
  84:         cost_usd=0.0,
  85:     )
  86: 
  87: 
  88: def _kept(text: str, tokens: list[str]) -> VerifiedSentence:
  89:     return VerifiedSentence(
  90:         section_id="sec_x",
  91:         sentence_text=text,
  92:         provenance_tokens=tokens,
  93:         verifier_pass=True,
  94:     )
  95: 
  96: 
  97: def _section(*sentences: VerifiedSentence) -> Section:
  98:     return Section(
  99:         section_id="sec_x",
 100:         section_title="X",
 101:         verified_sentences=list(sentences),
 102:         section_verify_pass_rate=1.0 if sentences and all(s.verifier_pass for s in sentences) else 0.5,
 103:         section_status="verified",
 104:     )
 105: 
 106: 
 107: def _report(*sections: Section) -> VerifiedReport:
 108:     return VerifiedReport(
 109:         pool_id="pool",
 110:         decision_id="dec",
 111:         sections=list(sections),
 112:         overall_verify_pass_rate=1.0,
 113:         pipeline_verdict="success",
 114:         generator_model="m",
 115:         verifier_pass_threshold=0.4,
 116:         started_at_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
 117:         finished_at_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
 118:         latency_ms=120000,
 119:         cost_usd=0.0,
 120:     )

  26: def _stub_sign(payload: bytes) -> bytes:
  27:     digest = hashlib.sha256(payload).hexdigest()
  28:     return (
  29:         f"-----BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE-----\n# stub hash={digest}\n-----END PGP SIGNATURE-----\n"
  30:     ).encode("utf-8")

  34:     def stub_provider():

  40: def _payload(verdict: str = "success", pool_id: str = "pool-1") -> dict:
  41:     """Build a request body that satisfies the FK chain + verdict."""
  42:     iso = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
  43:     decision = {
  44:         "decision_id": "dec-1",
  45:         "status": "in_scope",
  46:         "scope_class": "clinical_efficacy",
  47:         "ambiguity_axes": [

  53:         },
  54:         "server_time_utc": iso,
  55:     }
  56: 
  57: 
  58: def _retrieval_response(adequate: bool = True) -> dict:
  59:     iso = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
  60:     return {
  61:         "error": False,
  62:         "pool": {
  63:             "pool_id": "pool-1",
  64:             "decision_id": "dec-1",
  65:             "sources": [],
  66:             "adequacy": {
  67:                 "is_adequate": adequate,
  68:                 "sources_per_tier": {"T1": 0, "T2": 0, "T3": 0},
  69:                 "min_required_per_tier": {"T1": 0, "T2": 0, "T3": 0},
  70:                 "failure_reason": None if adequate else "no sources",
  71:             },
  72:             "queries_executed": [],
  73:             "retrieval_started_at_utc": iso,
  74:             "retrieval_finished_at_utc": iso,
  75:             "latency_ms": 0,
  76:             "cost_usd": 0.0,
  77:         },
  78:         "server_time_utc": iso,
  79:     }
  80: 
  81: 
  82: def _generation_response(verdict: str = "success") -> dict:
  83:     iso = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
  84:     return {
  85:         "error": False,
  86:         "report": {
  87:             "report_id": "report-1",
  88:             "pool_id": "pool-1",

  90:             "sections": [],

  95:             "started_at_utc": iso,
  96:             "finished_at_utc": iso,
  97:             "latency_ms": 1000,
  98:             "cost_usd": 0.01,
  99:         },
 100:         "server_time_utc": iso,
 101:     }
 102: 
 103: 
 104: def _make_handler(routes: dict[str, dict | int]):
 105:     """Build a MockTransport handler that returns canned responses per path."""
 106: 
 107:     def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
 108:         path = request.url.path
 109:         if path.endswith("/api/audit-bundle/health"):
 110:             return httpx.Response(200, json={"status": "ok"})
 111:         spec = routes.get(path)
 112:         if isinstance(spec, int):
 113:             return httpx.Response(spec, json={"detail": "stubbed error"})
 114:         if spec is None:
 115:             return httpx.Response(404, json={"detail": "not stubbed"})
 116:         return httpx.Response(200, json=spec)
 117: 
 118:     return handler

   1: """FastAPI route for slice 004 audit-bundle export.
   2: 
   3: POST /api/audit-bundle — accepts a {decision, pool, report} triple
   4: (typically the slice 001 + 002 + 003 chain output) and streams back
   5: a GPG-signed audit_<bundle_id>.tar.gz file.
   6: 
   7: Mounted alongside the other slice routes in polaris_v6.api.app.
   8: """
   9: 
  10: from __future__ import annotations
  11: 
  12: import tempfile
  13: from pathlib import Path
  14: from typing import Any, Callable
  15: 
  16: from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
  17: from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
  18: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
  19: 
  20: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.bundle_builder import (
  21:     SignFn,
  22:     build_audit_bundle,
  23: )
  24: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.bundle_schema import ContentType
  25: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.manifest_builder import build_manifest_and_files
  26: from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import VerifiedReport
  27: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  28: from polaris_graph.scope.scope_decision import ScopeDecision
  29: 
  30: PREVIEW_CONTENT_TYPES: tuple[ContentType, ...] = (
  31:     "scope_decision",
  32:     "evidence_pool",
  33:     "verified_report",
  34:     "source_snapshot",
  35:     "metadata",
  36: )
  37: 
  38: router = APIRouter(tags=["audit-bundle"])
  39: 
  40: 
  41: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  42: # Dependencies
  43: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  44: 
  45: def get_sign_fn() -> SignFn | None:
  46:     """Returns the active GPG signer or None.
  47: 
  48:     None signals the orchestrator's sentinel default which raises and is
  49:     caught by the route -> HTTP 503. Tests override this dep; production
  50:     binds to a real GPGSigner via app.dependency_overrides at startup
  51:     when POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID is set.
  52:     """
  53:     return None
  54: 
  55: 
  56: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  57: # Request / response models
  58: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  59: 
  60: class AuditBundleRequest(BaseModel):
  61:     """POST body for /api/audit-bundle.
  62: 
  63:     Carries the full BPEI chain (decision + pool + report). The route
  64:     re-validates the FK chain consistency before building.
  65:     """
  66: 
  67:     decision: ScopeDecision = Field(description="slice 001 ScopeDecision")
  68:     pool: EvidencePool = Field(description="slice 002 EvidencePool")
  69:     report: VerifiedReport = Field(
  70:         description="slice 003 VerifiedReport (verdict=success required)"
  71:     )
  72: 
  73: 
  74: class AuditBundleErrorResponse(BaseModel):
  75:     """Body returned with HTTP 4xx/5xx when bundle cannot be assembled."""
  76: 
  77:     error: bool = True
  78:     code: str  # 'fk_chain_mismatch' | 'verdict_not_success' |
  79:                # 'cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot' |
  80:                # 'copyrighted_span_in_bundle' |
  81:                # 'gpg_unavailable' | 'sign_failed'
  82:     message: str
  83:     report_id: str | None = None
  84: 
  85: 
  86: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  87: # Routes
  88: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  89: 
  90: @router.post("/audit-bundle")
  91: def post_audit_bundle(
  92:     req: AuditBundleRequest,
  93:     sign_fn: SignFn | None = Depends(get_sign_fn),
  94: ) -> Any:
  95:     """Build + return a GPG-signed audit bundle as application/gzip.
  96: 
  97:     Returns the .tar.gz file as a streaming download.
  98:     """
  99:     if sign_fn is None:
 100:         raise HTTPException(
 101:             status_code=503,
 102:             detail={
 103:                 "error": True,
 104:                 "code": "gpg_unavailable",
 105:                 "message": (
 106:                     "GPG signer not configured. Set POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID in env "
 107:                     "and ensure the corresponding key is in the gpg keyring."
 108:                 ),
 109:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 110:             },
 111:         )
 112: 
 113:     # Build into a temp dir; FileResponse copies it to the wire.
 114:     tmp_dir = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix="polaris_audit_"))
 115:     try:
 116:         bundle_path = build_audit_bundle(
 117:             req.decision,
 118:             req.pool,
 119:             req.report,
 120:             output_dir=tmp_dir,
 121:             sign_fn=sign_fn,
 122:         )
 123:     except ValueError as exc:
 124:         # FK chain mismatch, verdict != success, cited-span unreachable, or copyrighted span
 125:         msg = str(exc)
 126:         if "copyrighted span" in msg:
 127:             code = "copyrighted_span_in_bundle"
 128:         elif "cited span unreachable" in msg:
 129:             code = "cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot"
 130:         elif "FK chain" in msg or "pool_id" in msg or "decision_id" in msg:
 131:             code = "fk_chain_mismatch"
 132:         else:
 133:             code = "verdict_not_success"
 134:         raise HTTPException(
 135:             status_code=400,
 136:             detail={
 137:                 "error": True,
 138:                 "code": code,
 139:                 "message": msg,
 140:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 141:             },
 142:         )
 143:     except RuntimeError as exc:
 144:         raise HTTPException(
 145:             status_code=502,
 146:             detail={
 147:                 "error": True,
 148:                 "code": "sign_failed",
 149:                 "message": str(exc),
 150:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 151:             },
 152:         )
 153: 
 154:     return FileResponse(
 155:         path=str(bundle_path),
 156:         filename=bundle_path.name,
 157:         media_type="application/gzip",
 158:     )
 159:

 161: @router.post("/audit-bundle/preview")
 162: def post_audit_bundle_preview(req: AuditBundleRequest) -> dict[str, Any]:
 163:     """Build the manifest only and return it for preview (no GPG, no tar)."""
 164:     if req.report.pool_id != req.pool.pool_id:
 165:         raise HTTPException(
 166:             status_code=400,
 167:             detail={
 168:                 "error": True,
 169:                 "code": "fk_chain_mismatch",
 170:                 "message": (
 171:                     f"FK chain mismatch: report.pool_id={req.report.pool_id!r}"
 172:                     f" != pool.pool_id={req.pool.pool_id!r}"
 173:                 ),
 174:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 175:             },
 176:         )
 177:     if req.report.decision_id != req.decision.decision_id:
 178:         raise HTTPException(
 179:             status_code=400,
 180:             detail={
 181:                 "error": True,
 182:                 "code": "fk_chain_mismatch",
 183:                 "message": (
 184:                     f"FK chain mismatch: report.decision_id="
 185:                     f"{req.report.decision_id!r} != decision.decision_id="
 186:                     f"{req.decision.decision_id!r}"
 187:                 ),
 188:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 189:             },
 190:         )
 191:     try:
 192:         manifest, _files_bytes = build_manifest_and_files(
 193:             req.decision, req.pool, req.report
 194:         )
 195:     except ValueError as exc:
 196:         msg = str(exc)
 197:         if "copyrighted span" in msg:
 198:             code = "copyrighted_span_in_bundle"
 199:         elif "cited span unreachable" in msg:
 200:             code = "cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot"
 201:         else:
 202:             code = "verdict_not_success"
 203:         raise HTTPException(
 204:             status_code=400,
 205:             detail={
 206:                 "error": True,
 207:                 "code": code,
 208:                 "message": msg,
 209:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 210:             },
 211:         )
 212:     breakdown = {ct: {"count": 0, "bytes": 0} for ct in PREVIEW_CONTENT_TYPES}
 213:     for entry in manifest.files:
 214:         slot = breakdown[entry.content_type]
 215:         slot["count"] += 1
 216:         slot["bytes"] += entry.size_bytes
 217:     return {
 218:         "preview_bundle_id": manifest.bundle_id,
 219:         "generator_model": manifest.generator_model,
 220:         "polaris_version": manifest.polaris_version,
 221:         "file_count": len(manifest.files),
 222:         "total_bytes": manifest.total_bytes(),
 223:         "content_type_breakdown": breakdown,
 224:     }
