 succeeded in 2826ms:
   1: """FastAPI HTTP route for slice 003 generation pipeline.
   2: 
   3: POST /api/generation — accepts an EvidencePool (typically the slice 002
   4: response) and returns a VerifiedReport (HTTP 200) or GenerationError
   5: detail (HTTP 400).
   6: 
   7: Mirrors slice 001 intake_route.py + slice 002 retrieval_route.py.
   8: 
   9: Mount:
  10:     from polaris_graph.api.generation_route import router as generation_router
  11:     app.include_router(generation_router, prefix="/api")
  12: """
  13: 
  14: from __future__ import annotations
  15: 
  16: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  17: from typing import Any
  18: 
  19: from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
  20: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
  21: 
  22: from polaris_graph.evidence_contract import (
  23:     ContractRequiredError,
  24:     EvidenceContract,
  25:     assert_generation_has_contract,
  26:     evaluate_contract,
  27: )
  28: from polaris_graph.generator2.generator import (
  29:     GeneratorCompletionFn,
  30:     process_generation,
  31: )
  32: from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import (
  33:     GenerationError,
  34:     VerifiedReport,
  35: )
  36: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  37: 
  38: router = APIRouter(tags=["generation"])
  39: 
  40: 
  41: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  42: # Dependency: completion_fn injection
  43: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  44: 
  45: def get_completion_fn() -> GeneratorCompletionFn | None:
  46:     """Returns the active completion_fn or None.
  47: 
  48:     None signals process_generation() to use its default sentinel which
  49:     triggers GenerationError(completion_backend_unavailable). Tests
  50:     override this dep; PR 7 will replace the production default with the
  51:     real OpenRouter-backed adapter.
  52:     """
  53:     return None
  54: 
  55: 
  56: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  57: # Request / response models
  58: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  59: 
  60: class GenerationRequest(BaseModel):
  61:     """POST body for /api/generation.
  62: 
  63:     Accepts an EvidencePool verbatim (as returned by /api/retrieval).
  64:     Pydantic re-validates the structure on the way in so a malformed
  65:     pool yields HTTP 422 before the orchestrator runs.
  66: 
  67:     `scope_class` is OPTIONAL but recommended; without it the generator
  68:     falls back to the clinical_efficacy blueprint. Callers chaining
  69:     intake -> retrieval -> generation should thread the slice 001
  70:     ScopeDecision.scope_class through.
  71: 
  72:     `verifier_pass_threshold` overrides the default per-section pass-rate
  73:     threshold (default 0.40). Lower values let weaker sections through
  74:     (useful for early demos); higher values are stricter.
  75:     """
  76: 
  77:     pool: EvidencePool = Field(
  78:         description="EvidencePool from slice 002 retrieval (adequacy=True)"
  79:     )
  80:     scope_class: str | None = Field(
  81:         default=None,
  82:         description=(
  83:             "Optional clinical_* scope class to select the section "
  84:             "blueprint. Defaults to clinical_efficacy when omitted."
  85:         ),
  86:     )
  87:     verifier_pass_threshold: float | None = Field(
  88:         default=None,
  89:         ge=0.0,
  90:         le=1.0,
  91:         description=(
  92:             "Optional override for the per-section strict-verify pass "
  93:             "rate threshold. None -> use orchestrator default (0.40)."
  94:         ),
  95:     )
  96:     contract: EvidenceContract | None = Field(
  97:         default=None,
  98:         description=(
  99:             "Pre-generation Evidence Contract (I-ecg-001). Generation "
 100:             "REFUSES if missing AND POLARIS_REQUIRE_CONTRACT=1 — request "
 101:             "returns HTTP 400 with code 'contract_required'. Default OFF "
 102:             "for legacy callers during migration period; set env=1 in "
 103:             "production once all callers thread the contract."
 104:         ),
 105:     )
 106: 
 107: 
 108: class GenerationErrorResponse(BaseModel):
 109:     """Body returned with HTTP 400 when generation cannot proceed."""
 110: 
 111:     error: bool = True
 112:     code: str
 113:     message: str
 114:     pool_id: str | None = None
 115:     decision_id: str | None = None
 116: 
 117: 
 118: class GenerationSuccessResponse(BaseModel):
 119:     """Body returned with HTTP 200 wrapping a VerifiedReport.
 120: 
 121:     Note: a VerifiedReport with verdict='abort_no_verified_sections' is
 122:     still HTTP 200 (request succeeded; the corpus generated but every
 123:     section failed strict-verify; UI surfaces the abort verdict).
 124:     HTTP 400 is reserved for structural failures: inadequate input pool,
 125:     completion backend down, malformed output.
 126:     """
 127: 
 128:     error: bool = False
 129:     report: dict
 130:     server_time_utc: str
 131: 
 132: 
 133: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 134: # Routes
 135: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 136: 
 137: @router.post("/generation", response_model=None)
 138: def post_generation(
 139:     req: GenerationRequest,
 140:     completion_fn: GeneratorCompletionFn | None = Depends(get_completion_fn),
 141: ) -> GenerationSuccessResponse | GenerationErrorResponse:
 142:     """Run an EvidencePool through generator + strict-verify."""
 143:     import os
 144: 
 145:     require_contract = os.environ.get("POLARIS_REQUIRE_CONTRACT", "0").strip() == "1"
 146:     if require_contract:
 147:         try:
 148:             assert_generation_has_contract(req.contract, report_id=None)
 149:         except ContractRequiredError as exc:
 150:             raise HTTPException(
 151:                 status_code=400,
 152:                 detail={
 153:                     "error": True,
 154:                     "code": "contract_required",
 155:                     "message": str(exc),
 156:                     "pool_id": req.pool.pool_id,
 157:                     "decision_id": req.pool.decision_id,
 158:                 },
 159:             )
 160: 
 161:     kwargs: dict[str, Any] = {"scope_class": req.scope_class}
 162:     if req.verifier_pass_threshold is not None:
 163:         kwargs["verifier_pass_threshold"] = req.verifier_pass_threshold
 164:     if completion_fn is not None:
 165:         kwargs["completion_fn"] = completion_fn
 166:     result = process_generation(req.pool, **kwargs)
 167: 
 168:     if isinstance(result, GenerationError):
 169:         raise HTTPException(
 170:             status_code=400,
 171:             detail={
 172:                 "error": True,
 173:                 "code": result.code,
 174:                 "message": result.message,
 175:                 "pool_id": result.pool_id,
 176:                 "decision_id": result.decision_id,
 177:             },
 178:         )
 179: 
 180:     assert isinstance(result, VerifiedReport)
 181:     if require_contract and req.contract is not None:
 182:         verdict = evaluate_contract(req.contract, req.pool, result)
 183:         if not verdict.passed:
 184:             raise HTTPException(
 185:                 status_code=400,
 186:                 detail={
 187:                     "error": True,
 188:                     "code": "contract_unsatisfied",
 189:                     "message": (
 190:                         f"contract {req.contract.contract_id} unsatisfied: "
 191:                         f"{', '.join(verdict.failures)}"
 192:                     ),
 193:                     "pool_id": req.pool.pool_id,
 194:                     "decision_id": req.pool.decision_id,
 195:                 },
 196:             )
 197:     return GenerationSuccessResponse(
 198:         report=result.model_dump(mode="json"),
 199:         server_time_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z"),
 200:     )
 201:

 103: def _good_completion(text_per_call: list[str]) -> Callable:
 104:     state = {"i": 0}
 105: 
 106:     def fn(prompt, section_plan, pool):
 107:         i = state["i"]
 108:         state["i"] = i + 1
 109:         if i < len(text_per_call):
 110:             return text_per_call[i]
 111:         return text_per_call[-1] if text_per_call else ""
 112: 
 113:     return fn

 214: # Regeneration path
 215: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 216: 
 217: def test_first_attempt_fails_second_passes_marks_regenerated():
 218:     """First call returns token-less text (drops below threshold), second
 219:     returns valid text — section marked 'regenerated'."""
 220:     bad = "Aspirin works."
 221:     good = _good_efficacy_text()
 222: 
 223:     # 4 sections × 2 attempts each = 8 calls; first per section bad, second good
 224:     pattern = []
 225:     for _ in range(4):
 226:         pattern.append(bad)
 227:         pattern.append(good)
 228:     fn = _good_completion(pattern)
 229: 
 230:     result = process_generation(
 231:         _adequate_pool(),
 232:         completion_fn=fn,
 233:         scope_class="clinical_efficacy",
 234:     )

 325: 
 326: 
 327: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 328: # Parallel section execution
 329: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 330: 
 331: def test_sections_generated_in_parallel():
 332:     """The 4 sections must execute concurrently. Inject a completion_fn
 333:     that sleeps; verify total wall-clock < 4x serial time."""
 334:     import threading
 335:     import time as _time
 336: 
 337:     text = _good_efficacy_text()
 338:     SLEEP_S = 0.5
 339: 
 340:     call_lock = threading.Lock()
 341:     in_flight = {"current": 0, "max_concurrent": 0}
 342: 
 343:     def slow_fn(prompt, section_plan, pool):
 344:         with call_lock:
 345:             in_flight["current"] += 1
 346:             in_flight["max_concurrent"] = max(
 347:                 in_flight["max_concurrent"], in_flight["current"]
 348:             )
 349:         try:
 350:             _time.sleep(SLEEP_S)
 351:             return text
 352:         finally:
 353:             with call_lock:
 354:                 in_flight["current"] -= 1
 355: 
 356:     pool = _adequate_pool()
 357:     t0 = _time.perf_counter()
 358:     result = process_generation(
 359:         pool, completion_fn=slow_fn, scope_class="clinical_efficacy"
 360:     )
 361:     elapsed = _time.perf_counter() - t0
 362: 
 363:     assert isinstance(result, VerifiedReport)
 364:     # 4 sections × SLEEP_S serial = 2.0s; parallel should be ~SLEEP_S
 365:     # (one regen per section possible, so 2x sleep budget for safety).
 366:     assert elapsed < SLEEP_S * 3, (
 367:         f"parallel execution took {elapsed:.2f}s; "
 368:         f"expected < {SLEEP_S * 3:.2f}s (serial would be ~{SLEEP_S * 4:.2f}s)"
 369:     )
 370:     # At least 2 sections should have been in flight at the same time
 371:     assert in_flight["max_concurrent"] >= 2, (
 372:         f"max concurrent calls was {in_flight['max_concurrent']}; "
 373:         f"expected >= 2 for true parallelism"
 374:     )
 375: 
 376: 
 377: def test_section_order_preserved_after_parallel():
 378:     """Sections must come back in blueprint order regardless of which
 379:     finishes first."""
 380:     import time as _time
 381: 
 382:     text = _good_efficacy_text()
 383:     # Stagger sleeps so sections finish out of submit order
 384:     sleep_by_section = {
 385:         "sec_population": 0.05,
 386:         "sec_intervention": 0.30,
 387:         "sec_outcomes": 0.10,
 388:         "sec_limitations": 0.20,
 389:     }
 390: 
 391:     def staggered_fn(prompt, section_plan, pool):
 392:         _time.sleep(sleep_by_section.get(section_plan.section_id, 0.0))
 393:         return text
 394: 
 395:     result = process_generation(
 396:         _adequate_pool(),
 397:         completion_fn=staggered_fn,
 398:         scope_class="clinical_efficacy",
 399:     )
 400:     assert isinstance(result, VerifiedReport)
 401:     section_ids = [s.section_id for s in result.sections]
 402:     # Blueprint order: Population, Intervention, Outcomes, Limitations
 403:     assert section_ids == [
 404:         "sec_population",
 405:         "sec_intervention",
 406:         "sec_outcomes",
 407:         "sec_limitations",
 408:     ]

  55: 
  56: async function fulfill(page: Page, path: string, body: object, status = 200) {
  57:   await page.route(`**${path}`, async (route) => {
  58:     const method = route.request().method();
  59:     if (method === "OPTIONS") {
  60:       await route.fulfill({
  61:         status: 204,
  62:         headers: {
  63:           "access-control-allow-origin": "*",
  64:           "access-control-allow-methods": "POST,OPTIONS",
  65:           "access-control-allow-headers": "content-type",
  66:         },
  67:       });
  68:       return;
  69:     }
  70:     if (method !== "POST") return route.continue();
  71:     await route.fulfill({
  72:       status,
  73:       contentType: "application/json",
  74:       body: JSON.stringify(body),
  75:     });
  76:   });
  77: }
  78:

  43: export function GenerationRunner() {
  44:   const [question, setQuestion] = useState("");
  45:   const [show_dropped, setShowDropped] = useState(false);
  46:   const [state, setState] = useState<RunnerState>({ kind: "idle" });
  47: 
  48:   async function submit(e: React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>) {
  49:     e.preventDefault();
  50:     const trimmed = question.trim();
  51:     if (trimmed.length < 3) {
  52:       setState({
  53:         kind: "failed",
  54:         stage: "scope",
  55:         code: "too_short",
  56:         message: "Question is too short.",
  57:       });
  58:       return;
  59:     }
  60: 
  61:     setState({ kind: "loading", stage: "scope" });
  62:     let decision: IntakeScopeDecision;
  63:     try {
  64:       const intake = await runIntake(trimmed);
  65:       decision = intake.decision;
  66:     } catch (err) {
  67:       const code = err instanceof IntakeBadRequestError ? err.code : "unknown";
  68:       const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Intake failed.";
  69:       setState({ kind: "failed", stage: "scope", code, message: msg });
  70:       return;
  71:     }
  72: 
  73:     if (decision.status !== "in_scope") {
  74:       setState({
  75:         kind: "scope_unsuitable",
  76:         decision,
  77:         reason: scope_reason_for(decision),
  78:       });
  79:       return;
  80:     }
  81: 
  82:     setState({ kind: "loading", stage: "retrieval" });
  83:     let pool: EvidencePool;
  84:     try {
  85:       const retrieval = await runRetrieval(decision);
  86:       pool = retrieval.pool;
  87:     } catch (err) {
  88:       const code =
  89:         err instanceof RetrievalBadRequestError ? err.code : "unknown";
  90:       const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Retrieval failed.";
  91:       setState({ kind: "failed", stage: "retrieval", code, message: msg });
  92:       return;
  93:     }
  94: 
  95:     if (!pool.adequacy.is_adequate) {
  96:       setState({
  97:         kind: "failed",
  98:         stage: "retrieval",
  99:         code: "inadequate_pool",
 100:         message:
 101:           pool.adequacy.failure_reason ?? "Corpus not adequate for generation.",
 102:       });
 103:       return;
 104:     }
 105: 
 106:     setState({ kind: "loading", stage: "generation" });
 107:     try {
 108:       const generation = await runGeneration(pool, decision.scope_class);
 109:       setState({ kind: "ok", decision, pool, report: generation.report });

 112:         err instanceof GenerationBadRequestError ? err.code : "unknown";

 123:         </CardHeader>
 124:         <CardContent>
 125:           <form

 135:             </label>

 233: function DownloadAuditBundleButton({
 234:   decision,
 235:   pool,
 236:   report,
 237: }: {
 238:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision;
 239:   pool: EvidencePool;
 240:   report: VerifiedReport;
 241: }) {
 242:   const [dl_state, setDlState] = useState<DownloadState>({ kind: "idle" });
 243: 
 244:   async function handle_click() {
 245:     setDlState({ kind: "loading" });
 246:     try {
 247:       const blob = await downloadAuditBundle(decision, pool, report);
 248:       const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
 249:       const a = document.createElement("a");
 250:       a.href = url;
 251:       a.download = `audit_${report.report_id}.tar.gz`;
 252:       document.body.appendChild(a);
 253:       a.click();
 254:       document.body.removeChild(a);
 255:       URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
 256:       setDlState({ kind: "ok" });
 257:     } catch (err) {
 258:       if (err instanceof AuditBundleError) {
 259:         setDlState({ kind: "error", code: err.code, message: err.message });
 260:       } else {
 261:         const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Unknown error.";
 262:         setDlState({ kind: "error", code: "unknown", message: msg });
 263:       }
 264:     }
 265:   }
 266: 
 267:   if (dl_state.kind === "error") {
 268:     return (
 269:       <span
 270:         data-testid="audit-bundle-error"
 271:         className="text-xs text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
 272:         title={dl_state.message}
 273:       >
 274:         Bundle failed: {dl_state.code}
 275:       </span>
 276:     );
 277:   }
 278: 
 279:   return (
 280:     <button
 281:       type="button"
 282:       onClick={handle_click}
 283:       disabled={dl_state.kind === "loading"}
 284:       data-testid="download-audit-bundle"
 285:       className="text-foreground border-border bg-background hover:bg-muted rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
 286:     >
 287:       {dl_state.kind === "loading"
 288:         ? "Building bundle…"
 289:         : dl_state.kind === "ok"
 290:           ? "✓ Downloaded"
 291:           : "Download audit bundle"}
 292:     </button>
 293:   );
 294: }

 296: function stage_label(stage: RunnerStage): string {
 297:   switch (stage) {
 298:     case "scope":
 299:       return "Scope check";
 300:     case "retrieval":
 301:       return "Retrieval";
 302:     case "generation":
 303:       return "Generation";
 304:   }
 305: }
 306: 
 307: function scope_reason_for(decision: IntakeScopeDecision): string {
 308:   switch (decision.status) {
 309:     case "out_of_scope":
 310:       return "This question is out of scope for POLARIS clinical research.";
 311:     case "refused":
 312:       return "POLARIS refused this question (instruction-override attempt detected).";
 313:     case "ambiguous_needs_clarification":
 314:       return "This question is ambiguous. Clarify on the /intake page first.";
 315:     default:
 316:       return `Cannot generate for status='${decision.status}'.`;
 317:   }

  34: export function BundlePreview({
  35:   decision,
  36:   pool,
  37:   report,
  38: }: {
  39:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision;
  40:   pool: EvidencePool;
  41:   report: VerifiedReport;
  42: }) {
  43:   const [s, set_s] = useState<State>({ kind: "loading" });
  44:   useEffect(() => {
  45:     let cancel = false;
  46:     previewAuditBundle(decision, pool, report)
  47:       .then((preview) => {
  48:         if (!cancel) set_s({ kind: "ok", preview });
  49:       })
  50:       .catch((err: unknown) => {
  51:         if (cancel) return;
  52:         if (err instanceof AuditBundleError) {
  53:           set_s({ kind: "error", code: err.code, message: err.message });
  54:         } else {
  55:           const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Unknown error.";
  56:           set_s({ kind: "error", code: "unknown", message });
  57:         }
  58:       });
  59:     return () => {
  60:       cancel = true;
  61:     };
  62:   }, [decision, pool, report]);
  63: 
  64:   if (s.kind === "loading")
  65:     return (
  66:       <section
  67:         data-testid="bundle-preview-loading"
  68:         className="text-muted-foreground border-border rounded-md border p-3 text-xs"
  69:       >

  71:       </section>
  72:     );

  78:         title={s.message}
  79:       >
  80:         Bundle preview failed:{" "}
  81:         <span data-testid="bundle-preview-error-code">{s.code}</span>
  82:       </section>
  83:     );
  84:   const p = s.preview;
  85:   return (
  86:     <section
  87:       data-testid="bundle-preview"
  88:       className="border-border bg-muted/30 rounded-md border p-3 text-xs"
  89:     >
  90:       <header className="mb-2 flex flex-wrap gap-x-4 gap-y-1">
  91:         <span data-testid="bundle-preview-id">
  92:           Preview ID: {p.preview_bundle_id.slice(0, 8)}…
  93:         </span>
  94:         <span>Generator: {p.generator_model}</span>

   1: """Bundle manifest schema for slice 004 audit-bundle export.
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_004/architecture_proposal.md`.
   4: 
   5: Pure-types module. The BundleManifest is the audit anchor: an external
   6: verifier extracts the .tar.gz, computes SHA256 of every content file,
   7: checks against `files[*].sha256`, then verifies the GPG signature on the
   8: manifest itself. If the manifest verifies and content hashes match, the
   9: bundle is intact.
  10: """
  11: 
  12: from __future__ import annotations
  13: 
  14: import uuid
  15: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  16: from typing import Literal
  17: 
  18: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, field_validator
  19: 
  20: 
  21: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  22: # Type literals
  23: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  24: 
  25: ContentType = Literal[
  26:     "scope_decision",      # slice 001 ScopeDecision JSON
  27:     "evidence_pool",       # slice 002 EvidencePool JSON
  28:     "verified_report",     # slice 003 VerifiedReport JSON
  29:     "source_snapshot",     # full_text of one cited source
  30:     "metadata",            # bundle-level metadata (versions, etc.)
  31: ]
  32: 
  33: 
  34: BUNDLE_VERSION = "1.0"
  35: 
  36: 
  37: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  38: # FileEntry
  39: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  40: 
  41: class FileEntry(BaseModel):
  42:     """One file in the bundle, with hash anchor."""
  43: 
  44:     path: str = Field(
  45:         min_length=1,
  46:         max_length=500,
  47:         description=(
  48:             "Relative path inside the .tar.gz. e.g. 'manifest.yaml',"
  49:             " 'sources/abc-123.txt', 'verified_report.json'."
  50:         ),
  51:     )
  52:     sha256: str = Field(
  53:         min_length=64,
  54:         max_length=64,
  55:         description="Lowercase hex SHA256 digest of file contents.",
  56:     )
  57:     size_bytes: int = Field(ge=0)
  58:     content_type: ContentType
  59: 
  60:     @field_validator("sha256")
  61:     @classmethod
  62:     def _sha256_lowercase_hex(cls, v: str) -> str:
  63:         v = v.strip().lower()
  64:         if len(v) != 64:
  65:             raise ValueError("sha256 must be exactly 64 hex chars")
  66:         if any(c not in "0123456789abcdef" for c in v):
  67:             raise ValueError("sha256 must be lowercase hex")
  68:         return v
  69: 
  70:     @field_validator("path")
  71:     @classmethod
  72:     def _path_no_traversal(cls, v: str) -> str:
  73:         v = v.strip()
  74:         if v.startswith("/") or ".." in v.split("/"):
  75:             raise ValueError(
  76:                 "path must be relative and must not contain '..' segments"
  77:             )
  78:         return v
  79: 
  80: 
  81: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  82: # BundleManifest
  83: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  84: 
  85: class BundleManifest(BaseModel):
  86:     """Top-level bundle manifest — what GPG signs.
  87: 
  88:     The signature in `manifest.yaml.asc` is over the YAML-serialized form
  89:     of this manifest. External verifiers re-serialize and re-verify.
  90:     """
  91: 
  92:     bundle_id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
  93:     bundle_version: Literal["1.0"] = BUNDLE_VERSION
  94: 
  95:     # Foreign keys back through the BPEI spine
  96:     decision_id: str = Field(min_length=1, description="slice 001 ScopeDecision id")
  97:     pool_id: str = Field(min_length=1, description="slice 002 EvidencePool id")
  98:     report_id: str = Field(min_length=1, description="slice 003 VerifiedReport id")
  99: 
 100:     # Provenance metadata
 101:     generator_model: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
 102:     polaris_version: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=50)
 103: 
 104:     # Content files (excluding manifest.yaml + manifest.yaml.asc themselves)
 105:     files: list[FileEntry] = Field(default_factory=list, max_length=10000)
 106: 
 107:     bundle_created_at_utc: datetime = Field(
 108:         default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc)
 109:     )
 110: 
 111:     @field_validator("files")
 112:     @classmethod
 113:     def _files_unique_paths(cls, v: list[FileEntry]) -> list[FileEntry]:
 114:         paths = [f.path for f in v]
 115:         if len(set(paths)) != len(paths):
 116:             duplicates = sorted({p for p in paths if paths.count(p) > 1})
 117:             raise ValueError(
 118:                 f"files must have unique paths; duplicates: {duplicates}"
 119:             )
 120:         return v
 121: 
 122:     def file_by_content_type(
 123:         self, content_type: ContentType
 124:     ) -> list[FileEntry]:
 125:         """Filter files to a specific content_type. Used by verifiers."""
 126:         return [f for f in self.files if f.content_type == content_type]
 127: 
 128:     def total_bytes(self) -> int:
 129:         return sum(f.size_bytes for f in self.files)

 133: # BundleBuildError (parallel to other slices' Error types)
 134: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 135: 
 136: class BundleBuildError(BaseModel):
 137:     """Returned when a bundle cannot be assembled."""
 138: 
 139:     error: bool = True
 140:     code: str  # 'report_not_success' | 'gpg_unavailable' |
 141:                # 'gpg_key_missing' | 'serialization_failed'
 142:     message: str

   1: """Manifest builder — collects all bundle content + computes SHA256s.
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_004/architecture_proposal.md` §"manifest_builder".
   4: 
   5: Given a ScopeDecision + EvidencePool + VerifiedReport (the BPEI chain
   6: output), serializes each to canonical JSON, snapshots cited source
   7: texts, and assembles a BundleManifest with SHA256 anchors over every
   8: content file.
   9: 
  10: The manifest itself is YAML-serialized (canonical sort keys); GPG signs
  11: that YAML. External verifiers re-serialize the manifest and re-verify
  12: the signature.
  13: """
  14: 
  15: from __future__ import annotations
  16: 
  17: import hashlib
  18: import json
  19: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  20: from typing import Any
  21: 
  22: import yaml
  23: 
  24: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.bundle_schema import (
  25:     BUNDLE_VERSION,
  26:     BundleManifest,
  27:     FileEntry,
  28: )
  29: from pathlib import Path
  30: 
  31: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.snapshot_sources import (
  32:     snapshot_sources,
  33:     snapshot_sources_with_reachable,
  34: )
  35: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.sovereignty_guard import (
  36:     assert_all_pool_sources_legal_cleared,
  37: )
  38: from polaris_graph.generator2.provenance import extract_tokens
  39: from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import VerifiedReport
  40: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  41: from polaris_graph.scope.scope_decision import ScopeDecision
  42: 
  43: 
  44: POLARIS_VERSION = "6.2.0"
  45: 
  46: # Canonical filenames inside the bundle. External verifiers depend on
  47: # these; do not rename without bumping bundle_version.
  48: FILE_SCOPE_DECISION = "scope_decision.json"
  49: FILE_EVIDENCE_POOL = "evidence_pool.json"
  50: FILE_VERIFIED_REPORT = "verified_report.json"
  51: FILE_METADATA = "metadata.json"
  52: FILE_REVIEWER_README = "REVIEWER_README.md"
  53: SOURCES_DIR = "sources"
  54: 
  55: 
  56: def _sha256_bytes(data: bytes) -> str:
  57:     return hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest()
  58: 
  59: 
  60: def _serialize_json_canonical(model: Any) -> bytes:
  61:     """Pydantic model -> deterministic UTF-8 JSON bytes.
  62: 
  63:     sort_keys + no extra whitespace beyond standard separators ensures
  64:     re-serialization on the verifier side produces identical bytes →
  65:     SHA256 stable across implementations.
  66:     """
  67:     if hasattr(model, "model_dump"):
  68:         payload = model.model_dump(mode="json")
  69:     else:
  70:         payload = model
  71:     return json.dumps(
  72:         payload,
  73:         sort_keys=True,
  74:         ensure_ascii=False,
  75:         separators=(",", ":"),
  76:     ).encode("utf-8")
  77: 
  78: 
  79: def _assert_cited_spans_reachable(report: VerifiedReport, snapshots: dict) -> None:
  80:     """Raise ValueError if any cited span exceeds its snapshot's reachable_chars.
  81: 
  82:     Validates the UNION of tokens parsed from `sentence.sentence_text` and
  83:     `sentence.provenance_tokens`, deduped by `token.raw`. Missing source_id =>
  84:     unreachable. Span end > reachable_chars => unreachable.
  85:     """
  86:     seen: set[str] = set()
  87:     for section in report.sections:
  88:         if section.section_status == "dropped":
  89:             continue
  90:         for sentence in section.verified_sentences:
  91:             if not sentence.verifier_pass:
  92:                 continue
  93:             tokens = list(extract_tokens(sentence.sentence_text))
  94:             for raw in sentence.provenance_tokens:
  95:                 tokens.extend(extract_tokens(raw))
  96:             for tok in tokens:
  97:                 if tok.raw in seen:
  98:                     continue
  99:                 seen.add(tok.raw)
 100:                 entry = snapshots.get(tok.source_id)
 101:                 if entry is None:
 102:                     raise ValueError(
 103:                         f"cited span unreachable after snapshot: source "
 104:                         f"{tok.source_id!r} not in snapshots (token={tok.raw!r})"
 105:                     )
 106:                 if not (0 <= tok.span_start < tok.span_end <= entry.reachable_chars):
 107:                     raise ValueError(
 108:                         f"cited span unreachable after snapshot: source "
 109:                         f"{tok.source_id!r} token={tok.raw!r} span="
 110:                         f"{tok.span_start}-{tok.span_end} reachable={entry.reachable_chars}"
 111:                     )
 112: 
 113: 
 114: def _safe_source_filename(source_id: str) -> str:
 115:     """Build a tar-safe filename from a source_id.
 116: 
 117:     source_id is opaque (uuid by default, but could be 'src-1' etc). We
 118:     sanitize aggressively: only [a-zA-Z0-9_-]. Anything else becomes _.
 119:     Length-capped at 100 chars to avoid pathological inputs.
 120:     """
 121:     safe = "".join(
 122:         c if c.isalnum() or c in "-_" else "_" for c in source_id
 123:     )[:100]
 124:     return f"{SOURCES_DIR}/{safe}.txt"
 125: 
 126: 
 127: def build_manifest_and_files(
 128:     decision: ScopeDecision,
 129:     pool: EvidencePool,
 130:     report: VerifiedReport,
 131: ) -> tuple[BundleManifest, dict[str, bytes]]:
 132:     """Build the bundle manifest + content-file dict.
 133: 
 134:     Returns:
 135:         (manifest, files) where files is {path: content_bytes}. The
 136:         caller (bundle_builder) packs files into a tarball and writes
 137:         the manifest.yaml + manifest.yaml.asc alongside.
 138: 
 139:     Raises:
 140:         ValueError if report.pipeline_verdict != 'success'.
 141:     """
 142:     if report.pipeline_verdict != "success":
 143:         raise ValueError(
 144:             f"cannot build audit bundle for verdict "
 145:             f"{report.pipeline_verdict!r}; report must be successful"
 146:         )
 147: 
 148:     files_bytes: dict[str, bytes] = {}
 149: 
 150:     # 1. Slice 001 ScopeDecision
 151:     sd_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(decision)
 152:     files_bytes[FILE_SCOPE_DECISION] = sd_bytes
 153: 
 154:     # 2. Slice 002 EvidencePool
 155:     ep_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(pool)
 156:     files_bytes[FILE_EVIDENCE_POOL] = ep_bytes
 157: 
 158:     # 3. Slice 003 VerifiedReport
 159:     vr_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(report)
 160:     files_bytes[FILE_VERIFIED_REPORT] = vr_bytes
 161: 
 162:     # 4. Sovereignty: refuse to ship verbatim spans for non-cleared sources
 163:     assert_all_pool_sources_legal_cleared(pool)
 164: 
 165:     # 4b. Per-source snapshots + cited-span reachability guard
 166:     snapshot_entries = snapshot_sources_with_reachable(report, pool)
 167:     _assert_cited_spans_reachable(report, snapshot_entries)
 168:     for source_id, entry in snapshot_entries.items():
 169:         files_bytes[_safe_source_filename(source_id)] = entry.text.encode("utf-8")
 170:     snapshots = {sid: e.text for sid, e in snapshot_entries.items()}
 171: 
 172:     # 4b. REVIEWER_README ships verbatim in every bundle as metadata content_type.
 173:     readme_path = Path(__file__).parent / "REVIEWER_README.md"
 174:     files_bytes[FILE_REVIEWER_README] = readme_path.read_bytes()
 175: 
 176:     # 5. Bundle metadata (versions + creation timestamp)
 177:     metadata = {
 178:         "bundle_version": BUNDLE_VERSION,
 179:         "polaris_version": POLARIS_VERSION,
 180:         "created_at_utc": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat().replace(
 181:             "+00:00", "Z"
 182:         ),
 183:         "generator_model": report.generator_model,
 184:         "decision_id": decision.decision_id,
 185:         "pool_id": report.pool_id,
 186:         "report_id": report.report_id,
 187:         "source_snapshot_count": len(snapshots),
 188:     }
 189:     files_bytes[FILE_METADATA] = json.dumps(
 190:         metadata,
 191:         sort_keys=True,
 192:         ensure_ascii=False,
 193:         separators=(",", ":"),
 194:     ).encode("utf-8")
 195: 
 196:     # Build FileEntry list with content_type tags
 197:     file_entries: list[FileEntry] = []
 198:     content_type_by_path = {
 199:         FILE_SCOPE_DECISION: "scope_decision",
 200:         FILE_EVIDENCE_POOL: "evidence_pool",
 201:         FILE_VERIFIED_REPORT: "verified_report",
 202:         FILE_METADATA: "metadata",
 203:     }
 204:     for path, content in files_bytes.items():
 205:         ct = content_type_by_path.get(
 206:             path,
 207:             "source_snapshot" if path.startswith(SOURCES_DIR + "/") else "metadata",
 208:         )
 209:         file_entries.append(
 210:             FileEntry(
 211:                 path=path,
 212:                 sha256=_sha256_bytes(content),
 213:                 size_bytes=len(content),
 214:                 content_type=ct,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
 215:             )
 216:         )
 217: 
 218:     # Sort entries deterministically for stable manifest output
 219:     file_entries.sort(key=lambda f: f.path)
 220: 
 221:     manifest = BundleManifest(
 222:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
 223:         pool_id=report.pool_id,
 224:         report_id=report.report_id,
 225:         generator_model=report.generator_model,
 226:         polaris_version=POLARIS_VERSION,
 227:         files=file_entries,
 228:     )
 229:     return manifest, files_bytes
 230: 
 231: 
 232: def serialize_manifest_yaml(manifest: BundleManifest) -> bytes:
 233:     """Produce canonical YAML bytes for GPG signing.
 234: 
 235:     PyYAML default_flow_style=False + sort_keys=True keeps it stable
 236:     across re-serializations.
 237:     """
 238:     payload = manifest.model_dump(mode="json")
 239:     return yaml.safe_dump(
 240:         payload,
 241:         default_flow_style=False,
 242:         sort_keys=True,
 243:         allow_unicode=True,
 244:     ).encode("utf-8")

 succeeded in 1262ms:
 591: ### 9.1 Core Invariants (Non-Negotiable)
 592: 
 593: 1. **Two-family evaluator**: generator and evaluator MUST be from
 594:    different training lineages. `openrouter_client.check_family_segregation`
 595:    raises `RuntimeError` at construction if violated.
 596: 2. **Provenance tokens**: every generated sentence carries
 597:    `[#ev:<evidence_id>:<start>-<end>]` tokens. Sentences without valid
 598:    tokens are dropped by `strict_verify`.
 599: 3. **Strict verify**: per-sentence check enforces (a) evidence-id in pool,
 600:    (b) span bounds valid, (c) every decimal in sentence appears in span,
 601:    (d) sentence and span share ≥2 content words
 602:    (`PG_PROVENANCE_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP`). Fabricated claims fail at least
 603:    one of these.
 604: 4. **Zero-verified abort**: if every section fails strict_verify,
 605:    `report.md` is a pipeline-verdict artifact (not an empty-findings
 606:    pseudo-report). Status: `abort_no_verified_sections`.
 607: 5. **Corpus approval enforcement**: a corpus with material tier deviation
 608:    plus a rubber-stamp note aborts before any generator token is billed.
 609:    Status: `abort_corpus_approval_denied`.
 610: 6. **Budget cap holds even without `usage.cost`**: `_impute_cost_from_tokens`
 611:    backstops token-only responses. Negative tokens clamp to zero.
 612: 7. **Delimiter sanitization** (prompt-injection defense): evidence text
 613:    containing `<<<evidence:...>>>` or other delimiter literals —
 614:    including via NFKD/invisible-char/homoglyph evasions — is neutralized
 615:    before prompt wrapping. Byte-preserves legitimate multilingual content.
 616: 
 617: ### 9.2 Quality Gates (pipeline A)
 618: 
 619: | Gate | Threshold | Fail Action |
 620: |---|---|---|
 621: | Corpus adequacy | Min sources per tier (template-driven) | `abort_corpus_inadequate` |
 622: | Corpus approval | Auto-approved OR substantive operator note | `abort_corpus_approval_denied` |
 623: | Strict verify (per sentence) | Numeric match + ≥2 content-word overlap | Drop sentence |
 624: | Strict verify (per section) | ≥40% sentences verified | Attempt one regeneration |
 625: | Strict verify (pipeline) | At least one section with verified prose | `abort_no_verified_sections` |
 626: | Budget | Accumulated cost ≤ `PG_MAX_COST_PER_RUN` | `BudgetExceededError` |
 627: 
 628: ### 9.3 Pipeline verdict statuses (manifest.json)
 629: 
 630: | Status | Condition |
 631: |---|---|
 632: | `success` | All gates passed, generator produced verified prose |
 633: | `abort_scope_rejected` | Scope gate rejected the research question |
 634: | `abort_corpus_inadequate` | Corpus adequacy gate failed (not enough sources) |
 635: | `abort_corpus_approval_denied` | Corpus approval gate rejected (rubber-stamp note on material deviation) |
 636: | `abort_no_verified_sections` | Every generated section failed strict_verify |
 637: | `error_*` | Unexpected failure (API outage, malformed response, etc.) |
 638: 
 639: ### 9.4 Code hygiene (enforced by test suite, not a separate Sheriff)
 640: 
 641: **Forbidden patterns** (tests in `tests/polaris_graph/` detect these):
 642: 
 643: - `try: ... except: pass` without logging or re-raise (silent failure)
 644: - `import unittest.mock` or `from unittest.mock import ...` in `src/`
 645:   production code
 646: - Magic numbers (`if score > 0.7` instead of a named constant or env var)
 647: - `time.sleep()` to simulate work
